                <div class="abstract">
                    <div class="wrapper">
                        
                        
                        <div class="wrapper">
                            <h1 class="title">Baggage information</h1>
                            
                                <div class="description">
                                    
                                        <p>Your baggage allowance is listed on your e-ticket receipt and in <a href="/content/cx/en_US/manage-booking.html">Manage Booking</a>. Alternatively, you may use the calculator below to check your baggage allowance.</p>
<p>Note:</p>
<ul>
<li>If you have upgraded to a higher cabin using Upgrade Bid, your baggage allowance is still based on your original ticket allowance.</li>
<li>If your ticket involves flights marketed by other airlines, the baggage allowance may differ. Visit  <a href="/content/cx/en_US/baggage/check-in-baggage/carrier-rules.html">Carrier rules</a> for more details.</li>
</ul>

                                    
                                    
                                </div>
                            
                            
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
    

            
            
        
    
</div>

<div class="cmp-text margin-top-40">
    <h2>Pre-flight checklist</h2>
<p>Please take note of the following notes:</p>

</div>

    

	|









  




<div class="content-list">
  <div class="section-wrapper-bt section parbase  content-list-index-icon ">
    <div class="container   ">
      
      

      <div class="row equal-height">
        
        
          
            <div class="col-sm-12 col-md-6 col-lg-3 icon-list">
              <img class="icon" src="/content/dam/focal-point/digital-library/svg-icons/jade/stepper_1.svg" alt="Place sharp items into checked baggage">
              <div class="equal-height-watch content badge-inverted-white details" style="height: 327px;">
                <h3 class="title">Place sharp items into checked baggage</h3>
                <div class="description">
                  <p></p><p>If you are carrying nail scissors, letter knives or anything sharp and pointed, you will have to place them into checked baggage.</p>
<p></p>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
          
            <div class="col-sm-12 col-md-6 col-lg-3 icon-list">
              <img class="icon" src="/content/dam/focal-point/digital-library/svg-icons/jade/stepper_2.svg" alt="Check your luggage for prohibited items and items with restrictions">
              <div class="equal-height-watch content badge-inverted-white details" style="height: 327px;">
                <h3 class="title">Check your luggage for prohibited items and items with restrictions</h3>
                <div class="description">
                  <p></p><p>Depending on where you fly, there are restrictions on certain items and items which are prohibited to travel with entirely. For example, liquids, gases and aerosols are only allowed to be brought on board in certain volumes. Visit our <a href="/content/cx/en_US/baggage/controlled-and-banned-items/overview.html">restricted items</a> or more details.</p>
<p></p>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
          
            <div class="col-sm-12 col-md-6 col-lg-3 icon-list">
              <img class="icon" src="/content/dam/focal-point/digital-library/svg-icons/jade/stepper_3.svg" alt="Limit the amount of spare batteries you travel with">
              <div class="equal-height-watch content badge-inverted-white details" style="height: 327px;">
                <h3 class="title">Limit the amount of spare batteries you travel with</h3>
                <div class="description">
                  <p></p><p>Ensure that any spare batteries you travel with are stored properly and in acceptable amounts. Read more about travelling with <a href="/content/cx/en_US/baggage/controlled-and-banned-items/lithium-batteries.html">spare batteries</a>.</p>
<p></p>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
          
            <div class="col-sm-12 col-md-6 col-lg-3 icon-list">
              <img class="icon" src="/content/dam/focal-point/digital-library/svg-icons/jade/stepper_4.svg" alt="Be mindful of your luggage allowance">
              <div class="equal-height-watch content badge-inverted-white details" style="height: 327px;">
                <h3 class="title">Be mindful of your luggage allowance</h3>
                <div class="description">
                  <p></p><p>Check in any bags that are too heavy to lift into the overhead compartments.&nbsp; &nbsp;Our cabin crew are unable to lift or carry bags for you.&nbsp;</p>
<p>It is possible to travel with <a href="/content/cx/en_US/baggage/musical-instruments.html">musical instruments</a> and <a href="/content/cx/en_US/baggage/sports-equipment.html">sports equipment</a>, although please be aware rules differ according to your route. You can also check in <a href="/content/cx/en_US/baggage/extra-baggage-charges.html">extra baggage</a> for a small fee.</p>
<p></p>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
          
        
        

        
        
        

        
        
        
        
        
        
      </div>
    </div>
  </div>
</div>

            <div class="container  ">
				<div class="panel-group" id="ac5624e6a-696b-456f-b79b-974cd3426043_contentpar_accordion_copy" aria-multiselectable="false">

                            <span class="label">Travelling with smart bags</span>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-down"></i>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-up"></i>
						</a>
						<div id="ac5624e6a-696b-456f-b79b-974cd3426043_contentpar_accordion_copy-content" class="panel-collapse collapse" aria-labelledby="ac5624e6a-696b-456f-b79b-974cd3426043_contentpar_accordion_copy-title">

<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
    
    <div class="text parbase section aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div class="cmp-text">
    <ul>
<li>If you’re travelling with a smart bag, you must be able to remove the battery in case the bag has to be checked in at any point during the journey.</li>
<li>You must remove the lithium batteries and carry them in your cabin baggage. These will be treated in accordance with existing spare lithium battery requirements.</li>
</ul>
<p>For more details regarding baggage information, including controlled and banned items, please visit <a href="/content/cx/en_US/baggage/controlled-and-banned-items/lithium-batteries.html">travelling with spare batteries</a>.<br>
</p>

</div>

    

</div>

            <div class="container  ">
				<div class="panel-group" id="ac5624e6a-696b-456f-b79b-974cd3426043_contentpar_accordion_copy_copy" aria-multiselectable="false">
					 <div class="panel">
                     	<a class="panel-heading collapsed" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#ac5624e6a-696b-456f-b79b-974cd3426043_contentpar_accordion_copy_copy" href="#ac5624e6a-696b-456f-b79b-974cd3426043_contentpar_accordion_copy_copy-content" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="ac5624e6a-696b-456f-b79b-974cd3426043_contentpar_accordion_copy_copy-content" id="ac5624e6a-696b-456f-b79b-974cd3426043_contentpar_accordion_copy_copy-title">
                            <span class="label">Transfer baggage</span>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-down"></i>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-up"></i>
						</a>
						<div id="ac5624e6a-696b-456f-b79b-974cd3426043_contentpar_accordion_copy_copy-content" class="panel-collapse collapse" aria-labelledby="ac5624e6a-696b-456f-b79b-974cd3426043_contentpar_accordion_copy_copy-title">
							<div class="responsivegrid">


<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
    
    <div class="text parbase section aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div class="cmp-text">
    <p>We’ll be able to through-check your baggage to your final destination if you're:</p>
<ul>
<li>Holding connecting itineraries booked on a single ticket</li>
<li>Connecting between flights operated by Cathay Pacific</li>
<li>Travelling on separate tickets involving connections with our airline partners, provided that your journey begins with Cathay Pacific</li>
</ul>
<p>If you’re travelling to Australia or the US and transferring to a domestic flight, you may need to collect your baggage and clear customs before proceeding to your domestic connection.</p>
<p>Through-check may not be possible:</p>
<ul>
<li>If your travel begins with an airline that does not provide this service</li>
<li>Due to local customs restrictions and requirements</li>
</ul>

</div>

    

</div>

    
</div>

		<div class="section-wrapper-bt accordion-standard connected ">
            <div class="container  ">
				<div class="panel-group" id="ac5624e6a-696b-456f-b79b-974cd3426043_contentpar_accordion_copy_10697" aria-multiselectable="false">
					 <div class="panel">
                     	<a class="panel-heading collapsed" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#ac5624e6a-696b-456f-b79b-974cd3426043_contentpar_accordion_copy_10697" href="#ac5624e6a-696b-456f-b79b-974cd3426043_contentpar_accordion_copy_10697-content" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="ac5624e6a-696b-456f-b79b-974cd3426043_contentpar_accordion_copy_10697-content" id="ac5624e6a-696b-456f-b79b-974cd3426043_contentpar_accordion_copy_10697-title">
                            <span class="label">Items that qualify as a single piece of luggage</span>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-down"></i>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-up"></i>
						</a>
						<div id="ac5624e6a-696b-456f-b79b-974cd3426043_contentpar_accordion_copy_10697-content" class="panel-collapse collapse" aria-labelledby="ac5624e6a-696b-456f-b79b-974cd3426043_contentpar_accordion_copy_10697-title">
							<div class="responsivegrid">


<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
    
    <div class="text parbase section aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div class="cmp-text">
    <p>The following items&nbsp;can be checked in as one ‘piece’&nbsp;of baggage under your checked-baggage allowance.</p>
<ul>
<li>One sleeping bag or bed-roll</li>
<li>One rucksack, knapsack or backpack</li>
<li>One pair of snow skis with one pair of ski poles and boots</li>
<li>One snowboard and boots</li>
<li>One surf board (a maximum of 158cm / 62in in length)</li>
<li>One golf bag containing clubs and accompanying golf shoes</li>
<li>One duffle-type bag or type 22 bag (soft-sided and zippered bags with side panels that can be opened with a zipper)</li>
<li>One suitably packed bicycle. This should be: non-motorised touring or racing single seat bicycle; handlebars are fixed and tightened sideways or parallel to the frame or enclosed in plastic foam or similar material; pedals are removed or fixed inwards or enclosed in plastic foam or similar material; tyres are deflated; packed in a strong and protective hard case or recognised bicycle box.</li>
<li>One pair of standard water skis or slalom water skis</li>
<li>Suitably packed fishing equipment consisting of two rods, one reel, one landing net, one pair of fishing boots and tackle box</li>
</ul>
<p>Standard weight limitations apply to each item.</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p><b>Travelling with sporting firearms</b></p>
<p>Sporting firearms consist of:</p>
<ul>
<li>One rifle case containing not more than two rifles, 5kg / 10lb of ammunition, one shooting mat, noise suppressor and small rifle tools</li>
<li>Two shotguns and two shotgun cases</li>
<li>One pistol case containing no more than five pistols, 5kg / 10lb of ammunition, noise suppressors, one pistol telescope and small pistol tools</li>
</ul>
<p>Any passenger wishing to travel with firearms should read about our <a href="/content/cx/en_US/baggage/controlled-and-banned-items/banned-items.html">prohibited items</a> and <a href="/content/cx/en_US/contact-us.html">get in touch with your booking and reservation office</a> for further details.</p>

</div>

    

</div>

    
</div>
</div>

						</div>
					 </div>
				</div>
			</div>
		</div>

							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-down"></i>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-up"></i>

<div class="cmp-text">
    <p>Free baggage allowance and extra baggage charges for flights that involve one or more other airlines (i.e. not Cathay Pacific) rely on a new method of calculation. This is in agreement with the new baggage policy from the International Air Transport Association (IATA). Read more about our <a href="/content/cx/en_US/baggage/check-in-baggage/carrier-rules.html">most significant carrier rules</a>.</p>

</div>

    

</div>

            <div class="container  ">
				<div class="panel-group" id="ac5624e6a-696b-456f-b79b-974cd3426043_contentpar_accordion_1018044197" aria-multiselectable="false">
					 <div class="panel">
                     	<a class="panel-heading collapsed" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#ac5624e6a-696b-456f-b79b-974cd3426043_contentpar_accordion_1018044197" href="#ac5624e6a-696b-456f-b79b-974cd3426043_contentpar_accordion_1018044197-content" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="ac5624e6a-696b-456f-b79b-974cd3426043_contentpar_accordion_1018044197-content" id="ac5624e6a-696b-456f-b79b-974cd3426043_contentpar_accordion_1018044197-title">
                            <span class="label">Bringing mobility and assistive devices on board</span>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-down"></i>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-up"></i>
						</a>
						<div id="ac5624e6a-696b-456f-b79b-974cd3426043_contentpar_accordion_1018044197-content" class="panel-collapse collapse" aria-labelledby="ac5624e6a-696b-456f-b79b-974cd3426043_contentpar_accordion_1018044197-title">
							<div class="responsivegrid">


<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
    
    <div class="text parbase section aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div class="cmp-text">
    <p>If you use a mobility aid or assistive device to get around, we want to help you understand what you can bring free of charge. It depends on the nature of the device and the route you fly.</p>
<p>Acceptable items include portable electronic medical devices, canes, walkers, crutches, wheelchairs, and wheelchair accessories. Such devices help a passenger with a disability in their everyday life. Equipment used by a service animal (e.g. a harness or leash) that helps the animal work would also be considered an assistive device. Food for a service animal is not regarded as equipment and would have to be checked in or carried as hand baggage, following our regulations. Please note that wheelchairs are subject to stowage criteria.</p>
<p>Take note of your route to see what you can bring along free of charge.</p>
<p>For flights to/from the USA, there are no restrictions on the number of mobility aids and assistive aids you can bring on board for free.</p>
<p>On flights to other destinations, you may bring one assistive device and two mobility aids per passenger, in addition to your standard check in allowance.</p>
<p>Visit the <a href="/content/cx/en_US/prepare-trip/help-for-passengers.html">help for passengers</a> section for more details.</p>

</div>

    

</div>

    
</div>
</div>

<div class="contentpar parsys">




    
    
  
    
    
    <div class="text parbase section">
<div class="cmp-text margin-top-20">
    <h1>Check-in baggage allowance</h1>

</div>

    

</div>

    
  

    
    
  
    
    
    <div class="holder-fluid section">
    <div class="content-block section parbase   ">
    	
    	<div>


<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
    
    <div class="text parbase section aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div class="cmp-text margin-top-20 margin-bottom-40">
    <h2>What is my free checked baggage allowance?</h2>
<p>Please visit&nbsp;<a href="/content/cx/en_US/baggage.html">Baggage Information</a>&nbsp;page for details regarding your standard check-in allowance.&nbsp;</p>
<p>Please note that regardless of cabin class and Cathay status, we will not accept any single bag that is over 32 kg / 70 lbs in weight or 203 cm / 80 inch long in total dimension. The total dimension of your bag is the sum of its width, height, and length (L+W+H=203cm/80 inch). Baggage that exceeds the size and weight of your standard check-in allowance, or exceeds your Cathay or oneworld tier allowance, will require special handling and additional fees.&nbsp;</p>
<p>We have separate guidelines for non-standard baggage items, including musical instruments and sporting equipment.&nbsp;</p>

</div>

    

</div>
<div class="accordion parbase aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">


		<div class="section-wrapper-bt accordion-standard ">
            <div class="container  ">
				<div class="panel-group" id="aid_81312991-9915-4e86-8365-390402a82a1a_contentpar_colctrl_e883_responsivegrid_accordion_5232" aria-multiselectable="false">

                            <span class="label" role="heading" aria-level="noHeadingLevel">More about check-in baggage allowance</span>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-down"></i>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-up"></i>
						</a>

							<div class="responsivegrid">


<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
    
    <div class="parbase page-list section aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">

  
  
  
  
  
  
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
      
      	
    
    
    
    <div class="section-wrapper-bt page-list-plain">

    <script>
      // one trust banner
      const saveSelectionBtn = '#ot-pc-content > div.ot-pc-footer.details > div.ot-btn-container > button.save-preference-btn-handler.onetrust-close-btn-handler'
      const acceptAllBtn = '#ot-pc-content > div.ot-pc-footer > div.ot-btn-container > button.accept-recommended-btn-handler'
      const moreOptionsBtn = '#ot-pc-content > div.ot-pc-footer > div.ot-btn-container > div > button'

      function enableBodyScrolling() {
        document.documentElement.style.overflow = 'auto'
        const otBtnSaveSelection = document.querySelector(saveSelectionBtn)
        if (otBtnSaveSelection != null) { // only visible after clicked 'More options'
          otBtnSaveSelection.removeEventListener('click', enableBodyScrolling)
        }
        const otBtnAcceptAll = document.querySelector(acceptAllBtn)
        if (otBtnAcceptAll != null) {
          otBtnAcceptAll.removeEventListener('click', enableBodyScrolling)
        }
        const otBtnMoreOptions = document.querySelector(moreOptionsBtn)
        if (otBtnMoreOptions != null) {
          otBtnMoreOptions.removeEventListener('click', enableBodyScrolling)
        }
      }

      function disableBodyScrolling() {
        document.documentElement.style.overflow = 'hidden'
      }

      function addOtBtnSaveSelectionClickEvent() {
        const otBtnSaveSelection = document.querySelector(saveSelectionBtn)
        if (otBtnSaveSelection != null) { // only visible after clicked 'More options'
          otBtnSaveSelection.addEventListener('click', enableBodyScrolling)
        }
      }

      function addOtBtnAcceptAllClickEvent() {
        const otBtnAcceptAll = document.querySelector(acceptAllBtn)
        if (otBtnAcceptAll != null) {
          otBtnAcceptAll.addEventListener('click', enableBodyScrolling)
        }
      }

      function addOtBtnMoreOptionsClickEvent() {
        const otBtnMoreOptions = document.querySelector(moreOptionsBtn)
        if (otBtnMoreOptions != null) {
          otBtnMoreOptions.addEventListener('click', addOtBtnSaveSelectionClickEvent)
        }
      }

      // Select the node that will be observed for mutations
      let otEventInitialized = false
      const targetNode = document.body
      // Options for the observer (which mutations to observe)
      const config = {attributes: true, childList: true, subtree: true};
      // Callback function to execute when mutations are observed
      const callback = (mutationList) => {
        for (const mutation of mutationList) {
          if (mutation.type === 'childList' &&
            mutation.addedNodes.length > 0 &&
            mutation.addedNodes[0].id === 'onetrust-consent-sdk' &&
            !otEventInitialized
          ) {
            otEventInitialized = true
            const otBtnOpen = document.getElementById('ot-sdk-btn')
            otBtnOpen.addEventListener('click', () => {
              disableBodyScrolling()
              addOtBtnAcceptAllClickEvent()
              addOtBtnMoreOptionsClickEvent()
              addOtBtnSaveSelectionClickEvent()
            })
          }
        }
      };
      // Create an observer instance linked to the callback function
      const observer = new MutationObserver(callback);
      // Start observing the target node for configured mutations
      observer.observe(targetNode, config);
    </script>

    <div class="text parbase section">
<div class="cmp-text margin-top-20">
    <h1>Cabin baggage allowance<br>
</h1>

</div>

    

</div>

    
  

    
    
  
    
    
    <div class="holder-fluid section">
    <div class="content-block section parbase   ">
    	
    	<div>


<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
    
    <div class="text parbase section aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div class="cmp-text margin-top-20 margin-bottom-40">
    <h2>What is my carry-on baggage allowance?</h2>
<p>Customers with a reserved seat are entitled to one piece of carry-on luggage and one additional small item, which includes small handbags, laptop bags, small backpacks, camera bags or briefcases. You may also carry other necessary items such as a small camera or a walking stick on board. Please refer to <a href="/content/cx/en_US/travel-information/baggage/cabin-baggage.html">Baggage information</a> for further details.</p>

</div>

    

</div>
<div class="accordion parbase aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">


		<div class="section-wrapper-bt accordion-standard ">
            <div class="container  ">
				<div class="panel-group" id="acf69fe0a-2b67-4369-b659-01894f79839b_contentpar_colctrl_e883_responsivegrid_accordion_5232" aria-multiselectable="false">
					 <div class="panel">
                     	<a class="panel-heading collapsed" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#acf69fe0a-2b67-4369-b659-01894f79839b_contentpar_colctrl_e883_responsivegrid_accordion_5232" href="#acf69fe0a-2b67-4369-b659-01894f79839b_contentpar_colctrl_e883_responsivegrid_accordion_5232-content" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="acf69fe0a-2b67-4369-b659-01894f79839b_contentpar_colctrl_e883_responsivegrid_accordion_5232-content" id="acf69fe0a-2b67-4369-b659-01894f79839b_contentpar_colctrl_e883_responsivegrid_accordion_5232-title">
                            <span class="label" role="heading" aria-level="noHeadingLevel">More about cabin baggage allowance</span>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-down"></i>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-up"></i>
						</a>
						<div id="acf69fe0a-2b67-4369-b659-01894f79839b_contentpar_colctrl_e883_responsivegrid_accordion_5232-content" class="panel-collapse collapse" aria-labelledby="acf69fe0a-2b67-4369-b659-01894f79839b_contentpar_colctrl_e883_responsivegrid_accordion_5232-title">
							<div class="responsivegrid">

      <h2 class="caption">Making a claim</h2>
      <div class="sub-heading">
        <p>If your bag is missing or if it has been damaged, please follow the procedures below to make a claim.</p>

      </div>

      <div class="row equal-height">
        
        
          
            <div class="col-sm-12 col-md-4 col-lg-4 icon-list">
              <img class="icon" src="/content/dam/focal-point/digital-library/svg-icons/jade/stepper_1.svg" alt="Report your problem">
              <div class="equal-height-watch content badge-inverted-grey details" style="height: 198px;">
                <h3 class="title">Report your problem</h3>
                <div class="description">
                  <p></p><p>In order to make a claim, ensure you have reported the case and received a report file reference from the baggage enquiry desk at your arrival airport. Our airport team will do all they can to resolve your case.</p>
<p></p>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
          
            <div class="col-sm-12 col-md-4 col-lg-4 icon-list">
              <img class="icon" src="/content/dam/focal-point/digital-library/svg-icons/jade/stepper_2.svg" alt="Submit your claim">
              <div class="equal-height-watch content badge-inverted-grey details" style="height: 198px;">
                <h3 class="title">Submit your claim</h3>
                <div class="description">
                  <p></p><p>If our airport team can’t resolve your case, please complete the <a href="/content/cx/en_US/baggage/lost-and-damaged-baggage/baggage-claim-form.html" target="_blank" class="cx-newpage-link">online baggage claim form<span class="sr-only">Open a new window</span><span class="icon-newpage" aria-hidden="true"></span></a> with more details about your itinerary and belongings.</p>
<p></p>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
          
            <div class="col-sm-12 col-md-4 col-lg-4 icon-list">
              <img class="icon" src="/content/dam/focal-point/digital-library/svg-icons/jade/stepper_3.svg" alt="Send supporting documents">
              <div class="equal-height-watch content badge-inverted-grey details" style="height: 198px;">
                <h3 class="title">Send supporting documents</h3>
                <div class="description">
                  <p></p><p>After you’ve submitted your claim, you’ll receive a confirmation email. Please send a copy of your receipt(s) and any other supporting document(s) to the contact provided in the email.</p>
<p></p>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
          
        
        

        
        
        

        
        
        
        
        
        
      </div>

                     	<a class="panel-heading collapsed" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#aid_2f6a56f5-8daa-4bcc-9e36-c4715634c97c_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion" href="#aid_2f6a56f5-8daa-4bcc-9e36-c4715634c97c_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion-content" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="aid_2f6a56f5-8daa-4bcc-9e36-c4715634c97c_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion-content" id="aid_2f6a56f5-8daa-4bcc-9e36-c4715634c97c_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion-title">
                            <span class="label">Notices of claim and baggage liability limitations</span>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-down"></i>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-up"></i>
						</a>
						<div id="aid_2f6a56f5-8daa-4bcc-9e36-c4715634c97c_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion-content" class="panel-collapse collapse" aria-labelledby="aid_2f6a56f5-8daa-4bcc-9e36-c4715634c97c_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion-title">
							<div class="responsivegrid">


<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
    
    <div class="text parbase section aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div class="cmp-text">
    <p><b>Notice of claim</b></p>
<p>If you wish to claim compensation for delayed or damaged baggage, please follow the procedure outlined under ‘Making a claim’.</p>
<p>Please note that if you have private insurance coverage for your baggage, a claim should also be lodged with your insurance company.</p>
<p><b>Notice of baggage liability limitations</b></p>
<p>Liability for loss, delay or damage to baggage is limited unless a higher value is declared in advance and additional charges are paid. Excess valuation may be declared on certain types of articles.</p>
<p>For many international journeys (including domestic portions of international journeys), the Warsaw Convention may apply with liability limits of 17 Special drawing rights per kilo for checked baggage and 332 Special drawing rights per passenger for unchecked baggage. In cases where the Montreal Convention applies to your journey, the applicable liability limit is 1,288 Special drawing rights per passenger for checked and unchecked baggage. (The value of Special drawing rights can fluctuate - please check <a target="_blank" href="http://www.imf.org/external/np/fin/data/rms_five.aspx" class="cx-newpage-link">current exchange rates<span class="sr-only">, Link opens in a new window operated by external parties and may not conform to the same accessibility policies as Cathay Pacific</span> <span class="icon-newpage"></span></a>.)</p>
<p>Except for checked or unchecked baggage carried in the course of international carriage as defined by the Warsaw or Montreal Convention, we are not liable, in any way whatever, for loss of, damage to or delay in the delivery of articles which you include in your baggage despite their inclusion being prohibited by our General conditions of carriage for passengers and baggage. Such items include, but are not limited to, fragile or perishable items, keys, artwork, cameras, money, jewellery, precious metals, silverware, medicines, drug, dangerous goods, commercial goods, odd-sized articles, negotiable papers, securities or other valuables, business documents, samples or passports and other identification documents.</p>
<p>Please refer to our <a target="_blank" href="https://www.cathaypacific.com/content/dam/cx/legal-and-privacy/general-conditions-of-carriage-for-passengers-baggage-en.pdf" class="cx-newpage-link">Cathay Pacific General conditions of carriage for passengers and baggage (PDF)<span class="sr-only">Open a new window</span><span class="icon-newpage"></span></a></p>
<p>All downloadable files on this page are in PDF (Portable Document Format) and can be viewed with Adobe Acrobat Reader. <a target="_blank" href="https://acrobat.adobe.com/us/en/products/pdf-reader.html" class="cx-newpage-link">Download at no cost from Adobe’s website.<span class="sr-only">, Link opens in a new window operated by external parties and may not conform to the same accessibility policies as Cathay Pacific</span> <span class="icon-newpage"></span></a></p>

</div>

    

</div>

    
</div>
</div>

						</div>

    	<div>


<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
    
    <div class="text parbase section aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div class="cmp-text">
    <div class="panels panels-reverse equal-height-watch"><p><b>Advisory warning for customers travelling to or transiting through Hong Kong</b><br>
<br>
In addition to firearms and ammunition as described on this page:</p>
<ul>
<li>Stun guns, tear gas sprays, knuckle dusters and extendable batons are also classified as banned items by the laws of Hong Kong, no matter if you are arriving or transiting through Hong Kong. Offenders are liable upon conviction to a fine of HKD100,000 and imprisonment for 14 years. For further information, please refer to the <a target="_blank" href="http://www.police.gov.hk/ppp_en/04_crime_matters/cpa/cpa_at_01.html" class="cx-newpage-link">Hong Kong Police<span class="sr-only">Open a new window</span><span class="icon-newpage" aria-hidden="true"></span></a> website.</li>
<li>From 1 February 2023, Cannabidiol (CBD) – commonly used in products such as oils, gels and candies – will be listed as a dangerous drug under the Dangerous Drugs Ordinance (DDO) by the laws of Hong Kong. Anyone found to be in possession, consumption, trafficking and/or manufacturing are liable upon conviction to a maximum fine of HKD5,000,000 and life imprisonment. For further information, please refer to the <a target="_blank" href="https://www.nd.gov.hk/en/CBD.html" class="cx-newpage-link">Narcotics Division, Security Bureau<span class="sr-only">Open a new window</span><span class="icon-newpage" aria-hidden="true"></span></a> website.</li>
</ul>
</div>

</div>

    

</div>
<div class="text parbase section aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div class="cmp-text margin-top-20">
    <div class="section-wrapper-bt"><div class="container"><div class="text parbase section"><h2>Controlled items<br>
</h2>
<p>There are certain items that you are welcome to bring on board provided you follow our guidelines. Because we only fly to airports with thorough security checks, your items will be confiscated if they do not meet the requirements. Please read carefully over our advice to ensure your luggage complies with the regulations.</p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="section-wrapper-bt"><div class="container"><div class="text parbase section"><h2><b>Rules for all baggage</b></h2>
<p>You may bring the following items in either your check in or cabin baggage, providing the guidelines are followed.</p>
</div>
</div>
</div>

</div>

    

</div>
<div class="accordion parbase aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">


		<div class="section-wrapper-bt accordion-standard connected ">
            <div class="container  ">
				<div class="panel-group" id="ac983a3c3-f5e1-431d-a541-cf0377397ac5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion" aria-multiselectable="false">

                     	<a class="panel-heading collapsed" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#ac983a3c3-f5e1-431d-a541-cf0377397ac5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion" href="#ac983a3c3-f5e1-431d-a541-cf0377397ac5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion-content" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="ac983a3c3-f5e1-431d-a541-cf0377397ac5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion-content" id="ac983a3c3-f5e1-431d-a541-cf0377397ac5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion-title">
                            <span class="label">Liquids, aerosols, gels, and powders</span>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-down"></i>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-up"></i>
						</a>
						<div id="ac983a3c3-f5e1-431d-a541-cf0377397ac5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion-content" class="panel-collapse collapse" aria-labelledby="ac983a3c3-f5e1-431d-a541-cf0377397ac5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion-title">

<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
    
    <div class="text parbase section aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div class="cmp-text">
    <p>While we do have universal standards, regulations on travelling with liquids, aerosols, gels, and powders in your cabin luggage may vary depending on your flight route. Please visit our <a href="/content/cx/en_US/baggage/controlled-and-banned-items/liquids-aerosols-and-gels.html">dedicated page</a> for more information, including regulations on Duty Free liquid items.</p>

					 <div class="panel">
                     	<a class="panel-heading collapsed" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#ac983a3c3-f5e1-431d-a541-cf0377397ac5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_2097904418" href="#ac983a3c3-f5e1-431d-a541-cf0377397ac5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_2097904418-content" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="ac983a3c3-f5e1-431d-a541-cf0377397ac5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_2097904418-content" id="ac983a3c3-f5e1-431d-a541-cf0377397ac5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_2097904418-title">

<div class="cmp-text">
    <p>Pack your commercial or lithium batteries in the safest way possible with our list of helpful tips and regulations.<br>
<a href="/content/cx/en_US/baggage/controlled-and-banned-items/lithium-batteries.html">See more about spare batteries</a></p>

<div class="accordion parbase aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">


		<div class="section-wrapper-bt accordion-standard connected ">
            <div class="container  ">
				<div class="panel-group" id="ac983a3c3-f5e1-431d-a541-cf0377397ac5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1505515429" aria-multiselectable="false">
					 <div class="panel">
                     	<a class="panel-heading collapsed" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#ac983a3c3-f5e1-431d-a541-cf0377397ac5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1505515429" href="#ac983a3c3-f5e1-431d-a541-cf0377397ac5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1505515429-content" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="ac983a3c3-f5e1-431d-a541-cf0377397ac5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1505515429-content" id="ac983a3c3-f5e1-431d-a541-cf0377397ac5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1505515429-title">
                            <span class="label">Alcohol</span>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-down"></i>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-up"></i>
						</a>
						<div id="ac983a3c3-f5e1-431d-a541-cf0377397ac5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1505515429-content" class="panel-collapse collapse" aria-labelledby="ac983a3c3-f5e1-431d-a541-cf0377397ac5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1505515429-title">
							<div class="responsivegrid">


<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
    
    <div class="text parbase section aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div class="cmp-text">
    <p>Bringing home a little treat from your holidays? You may bring alcoholic beverages back with you, as long as they are in their retail packaging, with an alcoholic content of 24-70%. Each passenger is entitled to a total net quantity of 5 litres per person, either in your checked or cabin baggage. If your drinks have 24% or less alcohol content, they are not governed by the prior restrictions. Please be aware that if you take alcoholic items in your hand luggage,&nbsp;<a href="/content/cx/en_US/baggage/controlled-and-banned-items/liquids-aerosols-and-gels.html">rules for liquids, aerosols and gases</a>&nbsp;still apply.</p>
<p>Note: Different countries have their local customs regulations for bringing alcoholic beverages into the country. You are advised to check with the relevant authorities of the country you are travelling to if you plan to carry alcohol beverages in your cabin or checked bag.</p>

</div>

    

</div>

    
</div>
</div>

						</div>
					 </div>
				</div>
			</div>
		</div>
</div>
<div class="accordion parbase aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">


		<div class="section-wrapper-bt accordion-standard connected ">
            <div class="container  ">
				<div class="panel-group" id="ac983a3c3-f5e1-431d-a541-cf0377397ac5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_229199786" aria-multiselectable="false">
					 <div class="panel">
                     	<a class="panel-heading collapsed" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#ac983a3c3-f5e1-431d-a541-cf0377397ac5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_229199786" href="#ac983a3c3-f5e1-431d-a541-cf0377397ac5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_229199786-content" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="ac983a3c3-f5e1-431d-a541-cf0377397ac5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_229199786-content" id="ac983a3c3-f5e1-431d-a541-cf0377397ac5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_229199786-title">
                            <span class="label">Alcohol-based disinfectant and sanitiser products</span>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-down"></i>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-up"></i>
						</a>
						<div id="ac983a3c3-f5e1-431d-a541-cf0377397ac5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_229199786-content" class="panel-collapse collapse" aria-labelledby="ac983a3c3-f5e1-431d-a541-cf0377397ac5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_229199786-title">
							<div class="responsivegrid">


<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
    
    <div class="contentlist parbase holder-fluid aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">









  




<div class="content-list">
  <div class="section-wrapper-bt section parbase  background-white content-list-index-icon ">
    <div class="container    background-white">
      
      

      <div class="row equal-height">
        
        
          
            <div class="col-sm-12 col-md-12 col-lg-12 icon-list">
              <img class="icon" src="/content/dam/focal-point/digital-library/svg-icons/jade/information.svg">
              <div class="equal-height-watch content badge-inverted-white details">
                
                <div class="description">
                  <p></p><p>Please note: Each country has their own regulations regarding alcohol-based disinfectants on board. Please check with the relevant authorities of the country you’re travelling to.</p>
<p></p>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
          
        
        

        
        
        

        
        
        
        
        
        
      </div>
    </div>
  </div>
</div>






    

</div>
<div class="text parbase section aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div class="cmp-text margin-top-20">
    <p>You may bring liquids, aerosols, and gels in your cabin luggage as long as they do not exceed a maximum volume of 100ml for each item. These should be carried in one resealable, transparent plastic bag no more than 1L in capacity per passenger.</p>
<p>Items exceeding stated amounts should be packed into your checked bags.&nbsp;The total net quantity must not exceed 2kg or 2L per passenger, and the net quantity of each single item must not exceed 0.5kg or 0.5L.</p>

</div>

    

</div>

    
</div>
</div>

						</div>
					 </div>

<div class="accordion parbase aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">


		<div class="section-wrapper-bt accordion-standard connected ">
            <div class="container  ">
				<div class="panel-group" id="ac983a3c3-f5e1-431d-a541-cf0377397ac5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1362589809" aria-multiselectable="false">
					 <div class="panel">
                     	<a class="panel-heading collapsed" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#ac983a3c3-f5e1-431d-a541-cf0377397ac5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1362589809" href="#ac983a3c3-f5e1-431d-a541-cf0377397ac5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1362589809-content" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="ac983a3c3-f5e1-431d-a541-cf0377397ac5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1362589809-content" id="ac983a3c3-f5e1-431d-a541-cf0377397ac5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1362589809-title">
                            <span class="label">Lighters and matches</span>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-down"></i>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-up"></i>
						</a>
						<div id="ac983a3c3-f5e1-431d-a541-cf0377397ac5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1362589809-content" class="panel-collapse collapse" aria-labelledby="ac983a3c3-f5e1-431d-a541-cf0377397ac5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1362589809-title">
							<div class="responsivegrid">


<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
    
    <div class="text parbase section aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div class="cmp-text">
    <p>With the exception of China, Bangladesh and India, a passenger can carry one small packet of safety matches or a cigarette lighter on one’s person, which is intended for use by the individual only.<br>
<br>
If you’re travelling to/from USA, you may not travel with torch lighters. Please refer to the <a target="_blank" href="http://www.tsa.gov/" class="cx-newpage-link">TSA website<span class="sr-only">, Link opens in a new window operated by external parties and may not conform to the same accessibility policies as Cathay Pacific</span><span class="icon-newpage" aria-hidden="true"></span></a> for more information.</p>
<p>Please note: lighter fuel and refills are classed as a&nbsp;<a href="/content/cx/en_US/baggage/controlled-and-banned-items/banned-items.html">banned item</a>.</p>

</div>

    

</div>

    
</div>
</div>

						</div>
					 </div>

<p><b>Banned fruit items</b></p>
<p>Please note that most fruit items may be carried into the cabin as long as they are within our cabin baggage limitation – with the exception of durian and jackfruit, which are universally banned in aircraft cabins.<br>
<br>

<p>These type of smart bags will not be considered as a portable electronic device (PED); their batteries will be handled as a power bank or <a href="/content/cx/en_US/baggage/controlled-and-banned-items/lithium-batteries.html">spare lithium battery</a>.</p>

<div class="cmp-text">
    <h2>Controlled items allowed in cabin baggage</h2>
<p>The following items&nbsp;cannot be packed in your checked baggage&nbsp;but&nbsp;are allowed in your hand baggage, provided you meet the requirements.</p>

            <div class="container  ">
				<div class="panel-group" id="ac983a3c3-f5e1-431d-a541-cf0377397ac5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1342170378" aria-multiselectable="false">
					 <div class="panel">
                     	<a class="panel-heading collapsed" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#ac983a3c3-f5e1-431d-a541-cf0377397ac5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1342170378" href="#ac983a3c3-f5e1-431d-a541-cf0377397ac5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1342170378-content" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="ac983a3c3-f5e1-431d-a541-cf0377397ac5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1342170378-content" id="ac983a3c3-f5e1-431d-a541-cf0377397ac5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1342170378-title">
                            <span class="label">Electronic cigarettes</span>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-down"></i>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-up"></i>
						</a>
						<div id="ac983a3c3-f5e1-431d-a541-cf0377397ac5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1342170378-content" class="panel-collapse collapse" aria-labelledby="ac983a3c3-f5e1-431d-a541-cf0377397ac5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1342170378-title">
							<div class="responsivegrid">


<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
    
    <div class="text parbase section aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div class="cmp-text">
    <p>An electronic cigarette (e-cigarette) often runs with a battery and simulates tobacco smoking using heated vapour. Each device has a heating element that creates smoke known as a personal vaporiser or electronic nicotine delivery system (ENDS). Electronic cigarettes can only be carried on board either on one’s person or in your cabin baggage. It must not be used on the plane and must not be placed in your checked luggage. Recharging electronic cigarettes or its batteries on board is not permitted.</p>
<p>Electronic cigarettes must be individually protected to prevent accidental activation.</p>
<p><b>Please note the import of electronic cigarettes into Hong Kong, India, Singapore and Taiwan is prohibited.</b> More details on specific e-cigarette bans for each of these countries can be found on our <a href="/content/cx/en_US/baggage/controlled-and-banned-items/banned-items.html">Banned items page</a>.</p>

</div>

    

</div>

    
</div>

                            <span class="label">Guns, firearms and other devices that discharge projectiles</span>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-down"></i>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-up"></i>
						</a>
						<div id="ac983a3c3-f5e1-431d-a541-cf0377397ac5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1918884050-content" class="panel-collapse collapse" aria-labelledby="ac983a3c3-f5e1-431d-a541-cf0377397ac5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1918884050-title">
							<div class="responsivegrid">


<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
    
    <div class="text parbase section aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div class="cmp-text">
    <p>Please check with the <a target="_blank" href="http://www.cad.gov.hk/english/for_travellers.html#restricted" class="cx-newpage-link">Civil Aviation Department<span class="sr-only">, Link opens in a new window operated by external parties and may not conform to the same accessibility policies as Cathay Pacific</span><span class="icon-newpage"></span></a> of Hong Kong and the <a target="_blank" href="http://www.police.gov.hk/ppp_en/04_crime_matters/cpa/cpa_at_01.html" class="cx-newpage-link">Hong Kong Police department<span class="sr-only">, Link opens in a new window operated by external parties and may not conform to the same accessibility policies as Cathay Pacific</span> <span class="icon-newpage"></span></a>; if you plan to put any of these items into your checked bags.</p>
<p>Devices&nbsp;capable (or appearing capable) of being used to cause serious injury by&nbsp;discharging a projectile, including:</p>
<ul>
<li>firearms of all types, such as pistols, revolvers, rifles, shotguns</li>
<li>toy guns, replicas and imitation firearms capable of being mistaken for real weapons</li>
<li>component parts of firearms, excluding telescopic sights</li>
<li>compressed air and CO2 guns, such as pistols, pellet guns, rifles and ball bearing guns</li>
<li>signal flare pistols and starter pistols</li>
<li>bows, cross bows and arrows</li>
<li>harpoon guns and spear guns</li>
<li>slingshots and catapults</li>
</ul>
<p>Any passenger planning to travel with firearms should get in touch with our&nbsp;<a href="/content/cx/en_US/contact-us.html">Customer Care team</a> for further details.</p>

<li>martial arts equipment with a sharp point or sharp edge</li>
<li>swords and sabres</li>
<li>Umbrellas*</li>
</ul>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>*only for flights departing from the Philippines</p>
<p><b>Please note</b> carrying certain knives without a reasonable excuse may be criminal offence. If you encounter a knife such as a butterfly, flick or lock knife of any length police assistance should be sought in line with local procedures.</p>

<div class="cmp-text">
    <h2>Controlled items requiring visual verification</h2>
<p>There are certain items that you are welcome to bring on board in your checked and/or cabin baggage. However our Customer Services team at the Airport will need to verify the items by sight before they travel to ensure they are packed securely.</p>

</div>
<div class="accordion parbase aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">


		<div class="section-wrapper-bt accordion-standard ">
            <div class="container  ">
				<div class="panel-group" id="ac983a3c3-f5e1-431d-a541-cf0377397ac5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_2042570686" aria-multiselectable="false">
					 <div class="panel">
                     	<a class="panel-heading collapsed" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#ac983a3c3-f5e1-431d-a541-cf0377397ac5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_2042570686" href="#ac983a3c3-f5e1-431d-a541-cf0377397ac5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_2042570686-content" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="ac983a3c3-f5e1-431d-a541-cf0377397ac5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_2042570686-content" id="ac983a3c3-f5e1-431d-a541-cf0377397ac5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_2042570686-title">
                            <span class="label">Items requiring visual verification before travel</span>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-down"></i>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-up"></i>
						</a>
						<div id="ac983a3c3-f5e1-431d-a541-cf0377397ac5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_2042570686-content" class="panel-collapse collapse" aria-labelledby="ac983a3c3-f5e1-431d-a541-cf0377397ac5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_2042570686-title">
							<div class="responsivegrid">


<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
    
    <div class="text parbase section aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div class="cmp-text">
    <ul>
<li><a href="/content/cx/en_US/baggage/sports-equipment.html">Ammunition</a> - in quantities not exceeding 5 kg (11 lb) gross weight per person for that person’s own use, excluding ammunition with explosive or incendiary projectiles</li>
<li><a href="/content/cx/en_US/baggage/sports-equipment.html">Avalanche rescue backpack</a></li>
<li>Camping stove and fuel container that have contained a flammable liquid fuel</li>
<li>Chemical agent monitoring equipment&nbsp;</li>
<li>Dry ice - in quantities not exceeding 2.5 kg (5 lb) per person</li>
<li>Mercury barometer or thermometer&nbsp;</li>
<li>Small non-flammable gas cylinders&nbsp;</li>
<li>Battery-powered <a href="/content/cx/en_US/prepare-trip/help-for-passengers/disability-and-mobility-assistance/mobility-assistance.html">wheelchairs</a> or other similar mobility devices with spillable batteries or with <a href="/content/cx/en_US/baggage/controlled-and-banned-items/lithium-batteries.html">lithium batteries</a></li>
<li><a href="/content/cx/en_US/baggage/controlled-and-banned-items/lithium-batteries.html">Lithium battery</a>-powered electronic devices, such as portable medical electronic devices, &nbsp;camcorders, cameras, laptop computers (hyperlink to #4)<ul>
<li>containing lithium-ion batteries exceeding 100wh but not exceeding 160wh or</li>
<li>containing lithium metal cells exceeding 2g but not exceeding 8g</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Security-type equipment containing <a href="/content/cx/en_US/baggage/controlled-and-banned-items/lithium-batteries.html">lithium batteries</a></li>
<li>Spare <a href="/content/cx/en_US/baggage/controlled-and-banned-items/lithium-batteries.html">lithium batteries</a><ul>
<li>exceeding 100wh but not exceeding 160wh or</li>
<li>exceeding 2g but not exceeding 8g&nbsp;</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>

</div>

    

</div>

    
</div>
</div>

						</div>
					 </div>
				</div>
			</div>
		</div>
</div>
<div class="text parbase section aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div class="cmp-text">
    <p>Please contact our <a href="/content/cx/en_US/contact-us.html">Customer Care</a>&nbsp;for further information, and at the airport, please ensure you let us know that you are carrying one of these items.&nbsp; Once we have checked that it is safe to fly, we will provide you with the necessary approvals.&nbsp;</p>

</div>

    

</div>
<div class="text parbase section aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div class="cmp-text">
    <div class="section-wrapper-bt"><div class="container"><div class="text parbase section"><h2>Confiscated items</h2>
<p>We don’t like having to say no to our customers, but we ask you to comply with the above regulations so your safety is not compromised.</p>
<p>Legally, we are not responsible or liable for items removed from passengers by airport security personnel. This is because they are acting in accordance with international and governmental regulations.</p>
<p>If you do have an item that is confiscated, we cannot guarantee its return to you. However, if the security personnel return the item to us, we are happy to store it for a total of 7 days for you to pick up. In the best case scenario, we would of course like to see all customers reunited with their confiscated items, and we do everything we can to make sure this is the case.</p>
</div>
</div>
</div>

</div>

    

</div>

    
</div>
