<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
    
    <div class="text parbase section aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div class="cmp-text">
    <div class="panels panels-reverse equal-height-watch"><p><b>Advisory warning for customers travelling to or transiting through Hong Kong</b><br>
<br>
In addition to firearms and ammunition as described on this page:</p>
<ul>
<li>Stun guns, tear gas sprays, knuckle dusters and extendable batons are also classified as banned items by the laws of Hong Kong, no matter if you are arriving or transiting through Hong Kong. Offenders are liable upon conviction to a fine of HKD100,000 and imprisonment for 14 years. For further information, please refer to the <a target="_blank" href="http://www.police.gov.hk/ppp_en/04_crime_matters/cpa/cpa_at_01.html" class="cx-newpage-link">Hong Kong Police<span class="sr-only">Open a new window</span><span class="icon-newpage" aria-hidden="true"></span></a> website.</li>
<li>From 1 February 2023, Cannabidiol (CBD) – commonly used in products such as oils, gels and candies – will be listed as a dangerous drug under the Dangerous Drugs Ordinance (DDO) by the laws of Hong Kong. Anyone found to be in possession, consumption, trafficking and/or manufacturing are liable upon conviction to a maximum fine of HKD5,000,000 and life imprisonment. For further information, please refer to the <a target="_blank" href="https://www.nd.gov.hk/en/CBD.html" class="cx-newpage-link">Narcotics Division, Security Bureau<span class="sr-only">Open a new window</span><span class="icon-newpage" aria-hidden="true"></span></a> website.</li>
</ul>
</div>

</div>

    

</div>
<div class="text parbase section aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div class="cmp-text margin-top-20">
    <div class="section-wrapper-bt"><div class="container"><div class="text parbase section"><h2>Banned items</h2>
<p>For the safety of all our customers, please ensure your bags do not contain any of the following banned items. Because we only fly to airports with thorough security checks, your items will be confiscated if they do not meet the requirements.</p>
<p>Please refer to the <a target="_blank" href="http://www.cad.gov.hk/english/dangerousgoods.html" class="cx-newpage-link">Hong Kong Civil Aviation Department's Dangerous Goods page<span class="sr-only">Open a new window</span><span class="icon-newpage" aria-hidden="true"></span></a> <span class="sr-only">, Link opens in a new window operated by external parties and may not conform to the same accessibility policies as Cathay Pacific</span>for guidance and further details.</p>
</div>
</div>
</div>

</div>

    

</div>
<div class="text parbase section aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div class="cmp-text">
    <div class="section-wrapper-bt"><div class="container"><div class="text parbase section"><h2>Rules for all baggage</h2>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<h3>Stunning devices</h3>
<p>You may not bring any stunning devices, designed specifically to stun or immobilise, onto the plane.</p>

</div>

    

</div>
<div class="accordion parbase aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">


		<div class="section-wrapper-bt accordion-standard ">
            <div class="container  ">
				<div class="panel-group" id="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion" aria-multiselectable="false">
					 <div class="panel">
                     	<a class="panel-heading collapsed" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion" href="#aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion-content" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion-content" id="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion-title">
                            <span class="label">Examples of stunning devices </span>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-down"></i>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-up"></i>
						</a>
						<div id="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion-content" class="panel-collapse collapse" aria-labelledby="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion-title">
							<div class="responsivegrid">


<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
    
    <div class="text parbase section aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div class="cmp-text">
    <p>Devices include:</p>
<ul>
<li>devices for shocking, such as stun guns, tasers and stun batons</li>
<li>animal stunners and animal killers</li>
<li>disabling and incapacitating chemicals, gases and sprays, such as mace, pepper sprays, capsicum sprays, tear gas, acid sprays and animal repellent sprays</li>
<li>electric stunning devices</li>
</ul>

</div>

    

</div>

    
</div>
</div>

						</div>
					 </div>
				</div>
			</div>
		</div>
</div>
<div class="text parbase section aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div class="cmp-text">
    <h3>Explosives and incendiary substances</h3>
<p>You may not bring any explosive item or incendiary substance when you travel. This includes devices capable of or those appearing capable of causing serious injury or posing a threat to the safety of the aircraft.</p>

</div>

    

</div>
<div class="accordion parbase aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">


		<div class="section-wrapper-bt accordion-standard ">
            <div class="container  ">
				<div class="panel-group" id="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_747191269" aria-multiselectable="false">
					 <div class="panel">
                     	<a class="panel-heading collapsed" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_747191269" href="#aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_747191269-content" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_747191269-content" id="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_747191269-title">
                            <span class="label">Examples of explosives and incendiary substances</span>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-down"></i>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-up"></i>
						</a>
						<div id="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_747191269-content" class="panel-collapse collapse" aria-labelledby="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_747191269-title">
							<div class="responsivegrid">


<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
    
    <div class="text parbase section aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div class="cmp-text">
    <ul>
<li>ammunition</li>
<li>blasting caps</li>
<li>detonators and fuses</li>
<li>replica or limitation explosive devices</li>
<li>munitions, fireworks,&nbsp;toy fireworks&nbsp;and flares</li>
<li>mines, grenades and other explosive military stores</li>
<li>fireworks and other pyrotechnics</li>
<li>smoke-generating canisters and cartridges</li>
<li>dynamite, gunpowder and plastic explosives</li>
</ul>

</div>

    

</div>

    
</div>
</div>

						</div>
					 </div>
				</div>
			</div>
		</div>
</div>
<div class="text parbase section aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div class="cmp-text">
    <h3>Flammable items</h3>
<p>You may not bring any flammable substances onto the aircraft. These include harmful gases, liquids like lighter fuel and flammable solids.</p>

</div>

    

</div>
<div class="accordion parbase aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">


		<div class="section-wrapper-bt accordion-standard ">
            <div class="container  ">
				<div class="panel-group" id="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1242769412" aria-multiselectable="false">
					 <div class="panel">
                     	<a class="panel-heading collapsed" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1242769412" href="#aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1242769412-content" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1242769412-content" id="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1242769412-title">
                            <span class="label">Examples of flammable items</span>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-down"></i>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-up"></i>
						</a>
						<div id="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1242769412-content" class="panel-collapse collapse" aria-labelledby="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1242769412-title">
							<div class="responsivegrid">


<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
    
    <div class="text parbase section aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div class="cmp-text">
    <ul>
<li>Camping gas, glazing torches and other harmful gases</li>
<li>Flammable liquids like lighter fluid, petrol and diesel</li>
<li>Paints, thinner and liquid adhesives</li>
<li>Flammable solids like non-safety matches, disposable BBQ and coal</li>
<li>Strike anywhere matches", charcoal, phosphorus and articles which are easily ignited</li>
<li>Flameless Ration Heater like Self-heating Meal Ready-to-Eat (MRE) and self-heating instant hotpot</li>
</ul>

</div>

    

</div>

    
</div>
</div>

						</div>
					 </div>
				</div>
			</div>
		</div>
</div>
<div class="text parbase section aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div class="cmp-text">
    <h3>Harmful materials</h3>
<p>You may not bring oxidisers, poisons, corrosives or hazardous materials onto the plane. Hazardous materials include radioactive, biological and chemical substances.</p>

</div>

    

</div>
<div class="accordion parbase aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">


		<div class="section-wrapper-bt accordion-standard ">
            <div class="container  ">
				<div class="panel-group" id="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1652572192" aria-multiselectable="false">
					 <div class="panel">
                     	<a class="panel-heading collapsed" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1652572192" href="#aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1652572192-content" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1652572192-content" id="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1652572192-title">
                            <span class="label">Examples of harmful materials</span>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-down"></i>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-up"></i>
						</a>
						<div id="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1652572192-content" class="panel-collapse collapse" aria-labelledby="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1652572192-title">
							<div class="responsivegrid">


<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
    
    <div class="text parbase section aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div class="cmp-text">
    <ul>
<li>Oxidising liquids or solids like bleach, bleaching powder and peroxides</li>
<li>Toxic and poisonous substances like pesticides, weed killer, arsenic and cyanides</li>
<li>Chemical and biological hazardous substances, including infectious materials, such as biological products</li>
<li>Compressed gases (flammable, non-flammable or poisonous) such as butane, propane, aqualung cylinders, lighter fuels or refills, aerosols, chemical irritant aerosols</li>
<li>Corrosive materials such as mercury (which may be contained in thermometers or blood pressure gauges), acids, alkalis and wet cell batteries</li>
<li>Corrosives (car or other wet batteries, mercury)</li>
<li>Radioactive materials</li>
</ul>

</div>

    

</div>

    
</div>
</div>

						</div>
					 </div>
				</div>
			</div>
		</div>
</div>
<div class="text parbase section aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div class="cmp-text">
    <h3>Dangerous items</h3>
<p>You may not travel with items and lithium-powered vehicles that could cause serious harm to other passengers. This includes any other substances that present danger inflight such as magnetised, offensive or irritating materials.</p>

</div>

    

</div>
<div class="accordion parbase aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">


		<div class="section-wrapper-bt accordion-standard ">
            <div class="container  ">
				<div class="panel-group" id="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1495391868" aria-multiselectable="false">
					 <div class="panel">
                     	<a class="panel-heading collapsed" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1495391868" href="#aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1495391868-content" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1495391868-content" id="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1495391868-title">
                            <span class="label">Examples of dangerous items</span>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-down"></i>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-up"></i>
						</a>
						<div id="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1495391868-content" class="panel-collapse collapse" aria-labelledby="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1495391868-title">
							<div class="responsivegrid">


<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
    
    <div class="text parbase section aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div class="cmp-text">
    <ul>
<li>Small vehicles powered by lithium ion batteries, such as the AirWheel, Solowheel, Hoverboard, and other self-balancing scooters and mini Segways</li>
<li>Attaché briefcases with installed alarm devices</li>
<li>Incorporate lithium batteries</li>
<li>Pyrotechnic material</li>
</ul>

</div>

    

</div>

    
</div>
</div>

						</div>
					 </div>
				</div>
			</div>
		</div>
</div>
<div class="text parbase section aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div class="cmp-text">
    <h3>E-cigarettes/e-liquids (Hong Kong, India, Singapore and Taiwan)</h3>
<p>Passengers are not permitted to import electronic cigarette devices and other similar or related products into Hong Kong, India, Singapore and Taiwan. Please check national regulations for specific details, which varies for each country.</p>

</div>

    

</div>
<div class="accordion parbase aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">


		<div class="section-wrapper-bt accordion-standard connected ">
            <div class="container  ">
				<div class="panel-group" id="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1007672569" aria-multiselectable="false">
					 <div class="panel">
                     	<a class="panel-heading collapsed" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1007672569" href="#aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1007672569-content" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1007672569-content" id="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1007672569-title">
                            <span class="label">More details about the electronic cigarette ban in Hong Kong</span>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-down"></i>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-up"></i>
						</a>
						<div id="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1007672569-content" class="panel-collapse collapse" aria-labelledby="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1007672569-title">
							<div class="responsivegrid">


<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
    
    <div class="text parbase section aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div class="cmp-text">
    <p>The Hong Kong SAR Government has imposed a ban on the importation, promotion, manufacture, sale or possession of alternative smoking products, heated tobacco products and herbal cigarettes. This also includes for personal use. Passengers beginning or ending their journey in Hong Kong must not carry these items in either their checked or carry-on baggage. Passengers transiting through Hong Kong are not affected.<br>
<br>
Please visit the <a target="_blank" href="https://www.taco.gov.hk/t/english/legislation/legislation_asp.html" class="cx-newpage-link">Tobacco and Alcohol Control Office<span class="sr-only">Open a new window</span><span class="icon-newpage" aria-hidden="true"></span></a> website for further details.</p>

</div>

    

</div>

    
</div>
</div>

						</div>
					 </div>
				</div>
			</div>
		</div>
</div>
<div class="accordion parbase aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">


		<div class="section-wrapper-bt accordion-standard connected ">
            <div class="container  ">
				<div class="panel-group" id="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1311610103" aria-multiselectable="false">
					 <div class="panel">
                     	<a class="panel-heading collapsed" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1311610103" href="#aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1311610103-content" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1311610103-content" id="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1311610103-title">
                            <span class="label">More details about the electronic cigarette ban in Taiwan</span>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-down"></i>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-up"></i>
						</a>
						<div id="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1311610103-content" class="panel-collapse collapse" aria-labelledby="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1311610103-title">
							<div class="responsivegrid">


<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
    
    <div class="text parbase section aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div class="cmp-text">
    <p>The Ministry of Health and Welfare in Taiwan has imposed a ban on&nbsp;electronic cigarette devices (e-cigarettes) and its liquids (e-liquids), as part of the&nbsp;Tobacco Hazards Prevention Act. As such, import of these products into Taiwan is not allowed.</p>
<p>Please visit the <a href="https://etaipei.customs.gov.tw/News_Content.aspx?n=0C17752E865E33BD&amp;sms=B4E63546A494169D&amp;s=0F6EE71DC77E24E9" target="_blank" class="cx-newpage-link">Taipei Customs website<span class="sr-only">Open a new window</span><span class="icon-newpage" aria-hidden="true"></span></a> for further details.</p>

</div>

    

</div>

    
</div>
</div>

						</div>
					 </div>
				</div>
			</div>
		</div>
</div>
<div class="accordion parbase aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">


		<div class="section-wrapper-bt accordion-standard connected ">
            <div class="container  ">
				<div class="panel-group" id="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1240757383" aria-multiselectable="false">
					 <div class="panel">
                     	<a class="panel-heading collapsed" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1240757383" href="#aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1240757383-content" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1240757383-content" id="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1240757383-title">
                            <span class="label">More details about the electronic cigarette ban in India</span>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-down"></i>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-up"></i>
						</a>
						<div id="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1240757383-content" class="panel-collapse collapse" aria-labelledby="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1240757383-title">
							<div class="responsivegrid">


<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
    
    <div class="text parbase section aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div class="cmp-text">
    <p>The Ministry of Health and Family Welfare, Government of India, has imposed a ban on electronic cigarettes (e-cigarettes), including all electronic nicotine delivery systems (ENDS), heat-not-burn products, e-hookahs and other similar devices, excluding those licensed under the Drugs and Cosmetics Act, 1940. As such, the import, export or transport of these items in India is not allowed.</p>

</div>

    

</div>

    
</div>
</div>

						</div>
					 </div>
				</div>
			</div>
		</div>
</div>
<div class="accordion parbase aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">


		<div class="section-wrapper-bt accordion-standard ">
            <div class="container  ">
				<div class="panel-group" id="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_302802235" aria-multiselectable="false">
					 <div class="panel">
                     	<a class="panel-heading collapsed" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_302802235" href="#aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_302802235-content" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_302802235-content" id="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_302802235-title">
                            <span class="label">More details about the electronic cigarette ban in Singapore</span>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-down"></i>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-up"></i>
						</a>
						<div id="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_302802235-content" class="panel-collapse collapse" aria-labelledby="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_302802235-title">
							<div class="responsivegrid">


<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
    
    <div class="text parbase section aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div class="cmp-text">
    <p>The Ministry of Health in Singapore has imposed a ban on electronic cigarette devices (e-cigarettes), including all electronic nicotine delivery systems (ENDS), heated tobacco products and e-liquids as part of the Tobacco (Control of Advertisements and Sale) Act, or TCASA. As such, import, distribution, sale, purchase, use and possession of these products in Singapore are prohibited.</p>
<p>Please visit the <a href="https://www.hsa.gov.sg/tobacco-regulation/overview" target="_blank" class="cx-newpage-link">Singapore Health Sciences Authority website<span class="sr-only">Open a new window</span><span class="icon-newpage" aria-hidden="true"></span></a> or the <a href="https://www.moh.gov.sg/news-highlights/details/faqs-on-e-cigarettes-vaporisers-and-heat-not-burn-tobacco-products" target="_blank" class="cx-newpage-link">Singapore Ministry of Health website<span class="sr-only">Open a new window</span><span class="icon-newpage" aria-hidden="true"></span></a> for further details.</p>

</div>

    

</div>

    
</div>
</div>

						</div>
					 </div>
				</div>
			</div>
		</div>

<div class="text parbase section aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div class="cmp-text">
    <h3>Animal products and EU travel</h3>
<p>As a broad rule, passengers are not permitted to bring any consignment of meat products or milk products into the EU, with the exception of powdered infant milk, baby food or special food or pet foodstuffs required for medical purposes.</p>

</div>

    

</div>
<div class="accordion parbase aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">


		<div class="section-wrapper-bt accordion-standard ">
            <div class="container  ">
				<div class="panel-group" id="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_722320395" aria-multiselectable="false">
					 <div class="panel">

                            <span class="label">See full rules and regulations</span>

							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-up"></i>
						</a>
						<div id="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_722320395-content" class="panel-collapse collapse" aria-labelledby="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_722320395-title">
							<div class="responsivegrid">


<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
    
    <div class="text parbase section aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div class="cmp-text">
    <p>Products of animal origin may carry pathogens that can cause infectious diseases in animals. To prevent the spread of disease and for the general safety of our passengers, we are obliged to follow the <a href="http://ec.europa.eu/food/animal/animalproducts/personal_imports/index_en.htm" target="_blank" class="cx-newpage-link">EUROPA guidelines <span class="sr-only">Open a new window</span><span class="icon-newpage" aria-hidden="true"></span></a>on animal health.</p>
<p>As a general rule, passengers are not allowed to bring any consignment of meat, meat products, milk or milk products into EU. Please note that passengers arriving from Croatia, The Faeroe Islands, Greenland or Iceland may bring under 10 kilograms of such products for personal consumption.</p>
<p>The notable exception to the above rule is travel with up to 2 kilograms of powdered infant milk, infant food, or special foods/special pet feed required for medical purpose. The items must meet the following special requirements:<br>
</p>
<ul>
<li>The product does not require refrigeration before consumption</li>
<li>It is a product of packaged proprietary brand</li>
<li>The packaging is not broken</li>
</ul>
<p>For fishery products (including fish and certain shellfish such as prawns, lobsters, dead mussels and dead oysters), passengers are allowed to bring in such products up to 20 kilograms in total, or one fish that weights 20 kilograms or over.</p>
<p>This excludes those arriving from the Faeroe Islands or Iceland who have no weight restrictions on transporting fishery products, provided they are for personal consumption.</p>
<p>For updates and more details, please visit the <a target="_blank" href="http://ec.europa.eu/food/animal/animalproducts/personal_imports/index_en.htm" class="cx-newpage-link">European Commission Food Safety website.<span class="sr-only">Open a new window</span><span class="icon-newpage" aria-hidden="true"></span></a></p>

</div>

    

</div>

    
</div>
</div>

						</div>
					 </div>
				</div>
			</div>
		</div>
</div>
<div class="text parbase section aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div class="cmp-text">
    <h3>Laser pointers and travel to Switzerland</h3>
<p>Passengers are not permitted to import or transit with dangerous laser pointers in Switzerland.</p>

</div>

    

</div>
<div class="accordion parbase aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">


		<div class="section-wrapper-bt accordion-standard ">
            <div class="container  ">
				<div class="panel-group" id="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_68587466" aria-multiselectable="false">
					 <div class="panel">
                     	<a class="panel-heading collapsed" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_68587466" href="#aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_68587466-content" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_68587466-content" id="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_68587466-title">
                            <span class="label">See full details of the Swiss laser pointer ban</span>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-down"></i>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-up"></i>
						</a>
						<div id="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_68587466-content" class="panel-collapse collapse" aria-labelledby="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_68587466-title">
							<div class="responsivegrid">


<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
    
    <div class="text parbase section aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div class="cmp-text">
    <p>From 1 June, 2019, Switzerland imposed a ban on the following dangerous classes of laser pointers: <b>1M, 2, 2M, 3R, 3B, and 4</b>.</p>
<p>Other non-standard markings, including class <b>3A, IIIA, or 1C laser</b> are also considered dangerous. A laser pointer will be considered dangerous and banned if it carries no decipherable marking indicating which laser class it belongs to, or if it carries no marking at all.</p>
<p>Passengers should note that possession, importing of, and transiting with, the above classes of lasers is forbidden. (Possession of class 2 is allowed until 1 June 2021.)</p>
<p>Non-hazardous laser pointers are not included in the ban – please refer to the <a target="_blank" href="/content/dam/focal-point/cx/baggage/swiss_laserpointerverbot_en.pdf" class="cx-newpage-link">PDF<span class="sr-only">Open a new window</span><span class="icon-newpage" aria-hidden="true"></span></a> or the <a target="_blank" href="https://www.bag.admin.ch/bag/en/home/gesund-leben/umwelt-und-gesundheit/strahlung-radioaktivitaet-schall/elektromagnetische-felder-emf-uv-laser-licht/laser-und-lasershows/laserpointer.html" class="cx-newpage-link">Federal Department of Home Affairs (FDHA), Swiss Confederation website<span class="sr-only">Open a new window</span><span class="icon-newpage" aria-hidden="true"></span></a> for further details.</p>

</div>

    

</div>

    
</div>
</div>

						</div>
					 </div>
				</div>
			</div>
		</div>
</div>
<div class="text parbase section aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div class="cmp-text">
    <h3>Confiscated items</h3>
<p>Please take a moment to read through our security notice regarding banned items.</p>

</div>

    

</div>
<div class="accordion parbase aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">


		<div class="section-wrapper-bt accordion-standard ">
            <div class="container  ">
				<div class="panel-group" id="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_865344802" aria-multiselectable="false">
					 <div class="panel">
                     	<a class="panel-heading collapsed" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_865344802" href="#aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_865344802-content" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_865344802-content" id="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_865344802-title">
                            <span class="label">Security notice</span>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-down"></i>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-up"></i>
						</a>
						<div id="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_865344802-content" class="panel-collapse collapse" aria-labelledby="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_865344802-title">
							<div class="responsivegrid">


<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
    
    <div class="text parbase section aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div class="cmp-text">
    <p>We don’t like having to say no to our customers, but we ask you to comply with the above regulations so your safety is not compromised.</p>
<p>Legally, we are not responsible or liable for items removed from passengers by airport security personnel. This is because they are acting in accordance with international and governmental regulations.</p>
<p>If you do have an item that is confiscated, we cannot guarantee its return to you. However, if the security personnel return the item to us, we are happy to store it for a total of 7 days for you to pick up. In the best case scenario, we would of course like to see all customers reunited with their confiscated items, and we do everything we can to make sure this is the case.</p>

</div>

    

</div>

    
</div>
</div>

						</div>
					 </div>
				</div>
			</div>
		</div>
</div>
<div class="text parbase section aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div class="cmp-text">
    <h3>15-inch MacBook Pro battery recall</h3>

</div>

    

</div>
<div class="accordion parbase aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">


		<div class="section-wrapper-bt accordion-standard ">
            <div class="container  ">
				<div class="panel-group" id="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1561373178" aria-multiselectable="false">
					 <div class="panel">
                     	<a class="panel-heading collapsed" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1561373178" href="#aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1561373178-content" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1561373178-content" id="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1561373178-title">
                            <span class="label">Notice regarding recalled 15-inch MacBook Pros battery</span>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-down"></i>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-up"></i>
						</a>
						<div id="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1561373178-content" class="panel-collapse collapse" aria-labelledby="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1561373178-title">
							<div class="responsivegrid">


<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
    
    <div class="text parbase section aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div class="cmp-text">
    <p>Apple has recalled certain 15-inch MacBook Pro models with Retina display, sold between September 2015 and February 2017. Defective batteries in these MacBook Pros can overheat and pose a fire safety risk.</p>
<p>We therefore request that passengers refrain from bringing any affected models onboard a Cathay Pacific operated flight until the battery has been verified as safe or replaced by the manufacturer.</p>
<p>To check if this affects your device, please visit the <a href="https://support.apple.com/en-hk/15-inch-macbook-pro-battery-recall" target="_blank" class="cx-newpage-link">Apple website<span class="sr-only">Open a new window</span><span class="icon-newpage" aria-hidden="true"></span></a> and enter your serial number.</p>

</div>

    

</div>

    
</div>
</div>

						</div>
					 </div>
				</div>
			</div>
		</div>
</div>
<div class="text parbase section aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div class="cmp-text">
    <h3>Power-Assisted Bicycles (PABs) and Motorised Personal Mobility Devices (PMDs)</h3>
<p>Passengers importing Power-Assisted Bicycles (PABs) and Motorised Personal Mobility Devices (PMDs) are required to obtain approval from the Land Transport Authority (LTA) before importing these devices into Singapore.</p>

</div>

    

</div>
<div class="accordion parbase aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">


		<div class="section-wrapper-bt accordion-standard ">
            <div class="container  ">
				<div class="panel-group" id="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_43348177" aria-multiselectable="false">
					 <div class="panel">
                     	<a class="panel-heading collapsed" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_43348177" href="#aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_43348177-content" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_43348177-content" id="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_43348177-title">
                            <span class="label">Examples of Power-Assisted Bicycles (PABs) and Motorised Personal Mobility Devices (PMDs)  </span>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-down"></i>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-up"></i>
						</a>
						<div id="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_43348177-content" class="panel-collapse collapse" aria-labelledby="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_43348177-title">
							<div class="responsivegrid">


<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
    
    <div class="text parbase section aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div class="cmp-text">
    <ul>
<li>Electric scooters</li>
<li>Hoverboards</li>
<li>Electric unicycles</li>
<li>Electric skateboards</li>
</ul>
<p>Please visit the <a href="https://go.gov.sg/pmdimport" target="_blank" class="cx-newpage-link">LTA website<span class="sr-only">Open a new window</span><span class="icon-newpage" aria-hidden="true"></span></a> for more details.<br>
<br>
Note: Passengers are not permitted to bring small vehicles running on lithium-ion batteries onto the aircraft. Please visit <a href="/content/cx/en_US/baggage/controlled-and-banned-items/lithium-batteries.html">Ban on hoverboards and other self-balancing scooters</a> for more information.</p>

<div class="text parbase section aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div class="cmp-text">
    <h3>Satellite phones (India)</h3>
<p>Passengers are not permitted to import satellite phones to India.</p>

</div>

    

</div>
<div class="accordion parbase aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">


		<div class="section-wrapper-bt accordion-standard ">
            <div class="container  ">
				<div class="panel-group" id="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1879568988" aria-multiselectable="false">
					 <div class="panel">
                     	<a class="panel-heading collapsed" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1879568988" href="#aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1879568988-content" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1879568988-content" id="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1879568988-title">
                            <span class="label">More details about importing satellite phones to India</span>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-down"></i>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-up"></i>
						</a>
						<div id="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1879568988-content" class="panel-collapse collapse" aria-labelledby="aid_7cd9deba-21a0-4289-a930-4c155604662b_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1879568988-title">
							<div class="responsivegrid">


<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
    
    <div class="text parbase section aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div class="cmp-text">
    <p>The Government of India has banned the importation of satellite phones without permission in either checked or carry-on baggage. Passengers transiting through India are not affected.</p>
<p>Visit the <a href="https://old.cbic.gov.in/htdocs-cbec/guide_for_travellers/guide-for-travellers" target="_blank" class="cx-newpage-link">Central Board of Indirect Taxes &amp; Customs<span class="sr-only">Open a new window</span><span class="icon-newpage" aria-hidden="true"></span></a> website for further details.</p>

</div>

    

</div>

    
</div>
</div>

                        <h1 class="title">Controlled and banned items</h1>
				  </div>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>

    <div class="holder-fluid section">
    <div class="content-block section parbase   ">
    	
    	<div>


<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
    
    <div class="text parbase section aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div class="cmp-text">
    <h2><b>Bringing liquids, aerosols, gels, and powders aboard</b></h2>
<p>You may bring liquids, aerosols, and gels in your cabin luggage as long as they do not exceed a maximum volume of&nbsp;<b>100ml</b>&nbsp;for each item, carried in one resealable, transparent plastic bag no more than 1-litre in capacity per passenger. See below for details.</p>
<p>There are security restrictions in the United States and Australia/New Zealand on the carriage of certain types of&nbsp;<b>powders</b>&nbsp;into the cabin of an aircraft, limiting maximum volume to&nbsp;<b>350ml (12oz)</b>. Please refer to Route exceptions below for further information.</p>
<p>Items exceeding stated amounts should be packed into your checked bags. Please note that airport security personnel will remove items that do not meet these requirements before you fly.</p>

</div>

    

</div>
<div class="parbase column-component section aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
	




	
	
    
    
    
    
	<div class="section-wrapper-bt">
		<div class="container ">
            <div class="row equal-height">
                <div class="col-sm-12 col-md-6 col-lg-6">
                    <div class="columns-component">       
                        <div class="responsivegrid">


<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
    
    <div class="image aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div data-cmp-is="image" data-cmp-lazythreshold="0" data-cmp-src="/content/cx/en_US/baggage/controlled-and-banned-items/liquids-aerosols-and-gels/_jcr_content/contentpar/contentblock/responsivegrid/columncontrol/column1/image.coreimg{.width}.jpeg/1704168870345/liquids-aerosels-and-gels.jpeg" data-asset="/content/dam/focal-point/cx/baggage/liquids_aerosels_and_gels.jpg" data-asset-id="1493ae98-39c5-4b55-bf5f-5af1b4775785" id="image-d79099b33a" class="cmp-image" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject">
    
        
            
            <img src="/content/cx/en_US/baggage/controlled-and-banned-items/liquids-aerosols-and-gels/_jcr_content/contentpar/contentblock/responsivegrid/columncontrol/column1/image.coreimg.jpeg/1704168870345/liquids-aerosels-and-gels.jpeg" class="cmp-image__image" itemprop="contentUrl" data-cmp-hook-image="image" alt="">
            
        
    
    
    
</div>

    

</div>

    
</div>
</div>

                    </div>
                </div>
                <div class="col-sm-12 col-md-6 col-lg-6">
                    <div class="columns-component">            
                        <div class="responsivegrid">


<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
    
    <div class="text parbase section aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div class="cmp-text">
    <h3>Packaging your items</h3>
<p>Please use a resealable, transparent plastic bag or clear case to transport your liquids:</p>
<ul>
<li>Must not exceed 20cm / 8in in height and width</li>
<li>Must be 1 litre in volume</li>
<li>Must be transparent and re-sealable</li>
<li>Items must fit inside comfortably</li>
<li>Bag must fasten when closed</li>
<li>One bag per passenger</li>
<li>Bag must be presented separately from hand baggage for security</li>
</ul>

</div>

    

</div>

    
</div>
</div>

                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
		</div>
     </div>




    

</div>
<div class="text parbase section aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div class="cmp-text">
    <h3>Types of item</h3>
<p>Please use the following types of liquid, gel or aerosol as a guide:</p>
<ul>
<li>Gels, like hair gel or shower gel</li>
<li>Lotions and liquids, like sun cream or roll-on deodorant</li>
<li>Pastes, like toothpaste or Vaseline (only when travelling with infants)</li>
<li>Pressurised foams and sprays, like shaving foam or pressurised deodorant</li>
<li>Foodstuffs, like water or yoghurt</li>
<li>Liquid cosmetics, like foundation or lip-gloss</li>
</ul>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<h3>Item exceptions</h3>
<p>The following items, intended for use during your trip, can be carried in hand baggage in quantities above 100ml, provided they are presented for inspection at security.</p>
<ul>
<li>Medicines that are essential for travel, like diabetic kits</li>
<li>Baby food, in paste or liquid form (if you are travelling with an infant)</li>
<li>Expressed breast milk, of breast feeding mothers travelling with or without their baby</li>
<li>Non-liquid cosmetics, like lipsticks, powder foundation and solid deodorant</li>
</ul>
<p><b>Please note</b>&nbsp;the above exemptions are subject to verification by security.</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<h3>Duty Free items</h3>
<p>You may bring any volume of liquid, aerosol and gel items purchased at Duty Free stores in your hand luggage, provided you keep your proof of purchase and kept in a sealed, tamper-evident bag. Please note that some Duty Free stores may not provide you with a sealed, tamper-evident bag on purchase.</p>
<h2>Route exceptions</h2>
<p>The following destinations have restrictions which may affect which liquids, aerosols, gels, or powders you may bring in your cabin baggage. Please be sure to check this list before you travel to ensure you pack them appropriately.</p>

</div>

    

</div>
<div class="accordion parbase aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">


		<div class="section-wrapper-bt accordion-standard connected ">
            <div class="container  ">
				<div class="panel-group" id="aid_75f143da-7beb-48e6-9e08-46010341ca54_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion" aria-multiselectable="false">
					 <div class="panel">
                     	<a class="panel-heading collapsed" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#aid_75f143da-7beb-48e6-9e08-46010341ca54_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion" href="#aid_75f143da-7beb-48e6-9e08-46010341ca54_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion-content" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="aid_75f143da-7beb-48e6-9e08-46010341ca54_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion-content" id="aid_75f143da-7beb-48e6-9e08-46010341ca54_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion-title">
                            <span class="label">Australia</span>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-down"></i>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-up"></i>
						</a>
						<div id="aid_75f143da-7beb-48e6-9e08-46010341ca54_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion-content" class="panel-collapse collapse" aria-labelledby="aid_75f143da-7beb-48e6-9e08-46010341ca54_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion-title">
							<div class="responsivegrid">


<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
    
    <div class="text parbase section aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div class="cmp-text">
    <h4>Flights from Australia</h4>
<p><b>Powders</b><br>
Passengers are permitted to carry a maximum of 12oz (350ml) of inorganic powders (for example: salt, sand, talcum powder and some types of make-up) in the cabin of aircraft flying from Australia. Passengers should remove and separate powders, liquids, aerosols and gels from their cabin baggage and place them separately in a tray for x-ray examination at security screening points when departing Australia.<br>
<br>
Items excluded from the 12oz (350ml) restriction include baby products used to care for and/or feed an infant/toddler, medical/therapeutic products and cremated remains. Duty-free powders are also excluded when contained inside of a sealed bag with proof of purchase attached.</p>

</div>

    

</div>

    
</div>
</div>

						</div>
					 </div>
				</div>
			</div>
		</div>
</div>
<div class="accordion parbase aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">


		<div class="section-wrapper-bt accordion-standard connected ">
            <div class="container  ">
				<div class="panel-group" id="aid_75f143da-7beb-48e6-9e08-46010341ca54_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_2069154757" aria-multiselectable="false">
					 <div class="panel">
                     	<a class="panel-heading collapsed" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#aid_75f143da-7beb-48e6-9e08-46010341ca54_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_2069154757" href="#aid_75f143da-7beb-48e6-9e08-46010341ca54_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_2069154757-content" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="aid_75f143da-7beb-48e6-9e08-46010341ca54_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_2069154757-content" id="aid_75f143da-7beb-48e6-9e08-46010341ca54_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_2069154757-title">
                            <span class="label">Bahrain</span>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-down"></i>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-up"></i>
						</a>
						<div id="aid_75f143da-7beb-48e6-9e08-46010341ca54_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_2069154757-content" class="panel-collapse collapse" aria-labelledby="aid_75f143da-7beb-48e6-9e08-46010341ca54_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_2069154757-title">
							<div class="responsivegrid">


<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
    
    <div class="text parbase section aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div class="cmp-text">
    <p>The restrictions on travel with liquids are the same as regular travel (listed above).</p>
<p>Passengers arriving in Bahrain without further connecting flights can purchase duty free liquid items in-flight on the last sector of their journey.</p>

</div>

    

</div>

    
</div>
</div>

						</div>
					 </div>
				</div>
			</div>
		</div>
</div>
<div class="accordion parbase aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">


		<div class="section-wrapper-bt accordion-standard connected ">
            <div class="container  ">
				<div class="panel-group" id="aid_75f143da-7beb-48e6-9e08-46010341ca54_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_230037087" aria-multiselectable="false">
					 <div class="panel">
                     	<a class="panel-heading collapsed" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#aid_75f143da-7beb-48e6-9e08-46010341ca54_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_230037087" href="#aid_75f143da-7beb-48e6-9e08-46010341ca54_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_230037087-content" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="aid_75f143da-7beb-48e6-9e08-46010341ca54_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_230037087-content" id="aid_75f143da-7beb-48e6-9e08-46010341ca54_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_230037087-title">
                            <span class="label">Canada</span>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-down"></i>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-up"></i>
						</a>
						<div id="aid_75f143da-7beb-48e6-9e08-46010341ca54_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_230037087-content" class="panel-collapse collapse" aria-labelledby="aid_75f143da-7beb-48e6-9e08-46010341ca54_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_230037087-title">
							<div class="responsivegrid">


<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
    
    <div class="text parbase section aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div class="cmp-text">
    <p>The restrictions on travel with liquids are the same as regular travel (listed above).</p>
<p>Passengers arriving in Canada without further connecting flights can purchase duty free liquid items in-flight on the last sector of their journey. Please note that if travelling between the USA and Canada in the last sector of your journey, you are permitted to carry liquids over 100ml on board.</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>

</div>

    

</div>

</div>

						</div>
					 </div>

<div class="accordion parbase aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">


		<div class="section-wrapper-bt accordion-standard connected ">
            <div class="container  ">
				<div class="panel-group" id="aid_75f143da-7beb-48e6-9e08-46010341ca54_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_600114790" aria-multiselectable="false">
					 <div class="panel">
                     	<a class="panel-heading collapsed" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#aid_75f143da-7beb-48e6-9e08-46010341ca54_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_600114790" href="#aid_75f143da-7beb-48e6-9e08-46010341ca54_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_600114790-content" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="aid_75f143da-7beb-48e6-9e08-46010341ca54_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_600114790-content" id="aid_75f143da-7beb-48e6-9e08-46010341ca54_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_600114790-title">
                            <span class="label">Chinese Mainland</span>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-down"></i>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-up"></i>

		<div class="section-wrapper-bt accordion-standard connected ">
            <div class="container  ">
				<div class="panel-group" id="aid_75f143da-7beb-48e6-9e08-46010341ca54_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1761463878" aria-multiselectable="false">
					 <div class="panel">
                     	<a class="panel-heading collapsed" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#aid_75f143da-7beb-48e6-9e08-46010341ca54_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1761463878" href="#aid_75f143da-7beb-48e6-9e08-46010341ca54_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1761463878-content" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="aid_75f143da-7beb-48e6-9e08-46010341ca54_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1761463878-content" id="aid_75f143da-7beb-48e6-9e08-46010341ca54_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1761463878-title">
                            <span class="label">New Zealand</span>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-down"></i>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-up"></i>
						</a>
						<div id="aid_75f143da-7beb-48e6-9e08-46010341ca54_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1761463878-content" class="panel-collapse collapse" aria-labelledby="aid_75f143da-7beb-48e6-9e08-46010341ca54_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1761463878-title">
							<div class="responsivegrid">


<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
    
    <div class="text parbase section aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div class="cmp-text">
    <h4>Flights to New Zealand</h4>
<p><b>Liquids</b><br>
The restrictions on travel with liquids are the same as regular travel (listed above) for&nbsp;<b>direct flights and connecting domestic flights only</b>. You may not bring any liquids on board when on an international connecting flight through New Zealand.</p>
<p>Jars of honey and fish oil supplements exceeding 100ml in total volume cannot be hand carried, and must be checked in.</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<h4>Flights from New Zealand</h4>
<p><b>Powders</b><br>
Passengers are permitted to carry a maximum of 12oz (350ml) of inorganic powders (for example: salt, sand, talcum powder and some types of make-up) in the cabin of aircraft flying from New Zealand. Passengers should remove and separate powders, liquids, aerosols and gels from their cabin baggage and place them separately in a tray for x-ray examination at security screening points when departing New Zealand.<br>
<br>
Items excluded from the 12oz (350ml) restriction include baby products used to care for and/or feed an infant/toddler, medical/therapeutic products and cremated remains. Duty-free powders are also excluded when contained inside of a sealed bag with proof of purchase attached.</p>

</div>

    

</div>

    
</div>
</div>

						</div>
					 </div>
				</div>
			</div>
		</div>
</div>

		<div class="section-wrapper-bt accordion-standard ">
            <div class="container  ">
				<div class="panel-group" id="aid_75f143da-7beb-48e6-9e08-46010341ca54_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1235392721" aria-multiselectable="false">
					 <div class="panel">
                     	<a class="panel-heading collapsed" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#aid_75f143da-7beb-48e6-9e08-46010341ca54_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1235392721" href="#aid_75f143da-7beb-48e6-9e08-46010341ca54_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1235392721-content" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="aid_75f143da-7beb-48e6-9e08-46010341ca54_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1235392721-content" id="aid_75f143da-7beb-48e6-9e08-46010341ca54_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1235392721-title">
                            <span class="label">United States</span>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-down"></i>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-up"></i>
						</a>
						<div id="aid_75f143da-7beb-48e6-9e08-46010341ca54_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1235392721-content" class="panel-collapse collapse" aria-labelledby="aid_75f143da-7beb-48e6-9e08-46010341ca54_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1235392721-title">
							<div class="responsivegrid">


<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
    
    <div class="text parbase section aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div class="cmp-text">
    <p><b>Powders</b><br>
Passengers are permitted to carry less than 12oz (350ml) of powder-like substances (for example: flour, sugar, ground coffee, spices) in the cabin of aircraft flying to the United States. Passengers will undergo additional security checks at the boarding gate in Hong Kong before departure (or Vancouver for passengers travelling on CX888 to New York).</p>
<p>Items excluded from the less than 12oz (350ml) restriction include baby formula, medication and human remains. Duty-free powders are also excluded when contained inside of a properly sealed Secure Tamper Evident Bag.</p>
