    <div class="holder-fluid section">
    <div class="content-block section parbase   ">
    	
    	<div>


<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
    
    <div class="text parbase section aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div class="cmp-text">
    <div class="section-wrapper"><div class="container"><div class="text parbase section"><h2>Travelling with spare batteries</h2>
<p>Spare batteries can cause fires if not carried properly.</p>
<p>All types of spare batteries (such as lithium batteries, Nickel Cadmium (Ni-Cad) and Alkaline) can be carried safely in your cabin baggage provided that they are adequately protected against short circuit. You can prepare them for travel by:</p>
<ul>
<li>Enclosing them in their original retail packaging OR</li>
<li>Taping over the terminals OR</li>
<li>Placing each battery in a separate plastic bag or protective pouch</li>
<li>Turning off batteries in all electronic equipment i.e. cameras, mobile phones and computers so they cannot be accidentally re-activated when in checked baggage</li>
</ul>
<p>Whether a lithium battery can be carried by air or not depends on its configuration and its Watt-hour (Wh) rating (for rechargeable lithium-ion/polymer batteries) or Lithium Content (LC) (for non-rechargeable lithium metal batteries). Because we only fly to airports with thorough security checks, your items will be confiscated if they do not meet the requirements.</p>
<p>For the safety of yourself and fellow passengers, please take note of our regulations, and read our further guidelines for travel with lithium batteries.</p>
<p>Refer to&nbsp;<a href="/content/cx/en_US/prepare-trip/help-for-passengers/medical-assistance/medical-devices.html">Medical Devices</a>&nbsp;for more information on Portable Medical Electronic Devices.</p>
</div>
</div>
</div>

</div>

    

</div>
<div class="accordion parbase aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">


		<div class="section-wrapper-bt accordion-standard ">
            <div class="container  ">
				<div class="panel-group" id="aid_10ffc80a-0789-48a3-a8e0-8ef3152935a5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion" aria-multiselectable="false">
					 <div class="panel">
                     	<a class="panel-heading collapsed" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#aid_10ffc80a-0789-48a3-a8e0-8ef3152935a5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion" href="#aid_10ffc80a-0789-48a3-a8e0-8ef3152935a5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion-content" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="aid_10ffc80a-0789-48a3-a8e0-8ef3152935a5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion-content" id="aid_10ffc80a-0789-48a3-a8e0-8ef3152935a5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion-title">
                            <span class="label">Travelling with smart bags</span>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-down"></i>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-up"></i>
						</a>
						<div id="aid_10ffc80a-0789-48a3-a8e0-8ef3152935a5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion-content" class="panel-collapse collapse" aria-labelledby="aid_10ffc80a-0789-48a3-a8e0-8ef3152935a5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion-title">
							<div class="responsivegrid">


<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
    
    <div class="text parbase section aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div class="cmp-text">
    <p>From&nbsp;<b>1 January 2018</b>, smart bags with integrated lithium batteries for the purpose of charging an external device or to provide power to the wheels of the bag with non-removable lithium batteries will not be accepted as cabin or checked baggage.<br>
<br>
These type of smart bags will not be considered as a portable electronic device (PED); their batteries will be handled as a power bank or spare lithium battery.</p>
<p><u style="">Checked baggage</u><br>
</p>
<ul>
<li>If you travel with a smart bag, you must be able to remove the battery in case the bag has to be checked-in at any point during the journey.</li>
<li>You must carry the removed lithium battery in your cabin baggage and it will be treated in accordance with existing spare lithium battery requirements.</li>
</ul>
<p><u>Cabin baggage</u></p>
<ul>
<li>If you would like to take the smart bag as cabin baggage, the battery must be removable and should remain installed inside the bag.</li>
<li>If the battery cannot be removed, the bag will not be permitted for carriage as checked or cabin baggage.</li>
</ul>
<p>We recommend passengers check with operating carriers on connecting flights, for their policy regarding batteries and smart bags.<br>
</p>

</div>

    

</div>

    
</div>
</div>

						</div>
					 </div>
				</div>
			</div>
		</div>
</div>
<div class="contentlist parbase holder-fluid aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">









  




<div class="content-list">
  <div class="section-wrapper section parbase  content-list-image ">
    <div class="container   ">
      
      

      <div class="row equal-height">
        
        
        

        
        
        

        
        
          
            

            <div class="col-sm-12 col-md-4 col-lg-4">
              <div class="item">
                
                <div class="image-column">
                  <span data-picture="" data-role="presentation" data-alt="Small lithium batteries">
                    <span data-src="/content/dam/focal-point/cx/baggage/Small_lithium_batteries.renditionimage.900.600.jpg"></span>
                    
                    <span data-src="/content/dam/focal-point/cx/baggage/Small_lithium_batteries.renditionimage.900.600.jpg" data-media="(min-width: 720px)" style="background-image: url('/content/dam/focal-point/cx/baggage/Small_lithium_batteries.renditionimage.900.600.jpg');"></span>
                    <span data-src="/content/dam/focal-point/cx/baggage/Small_lithium_batteries.renditionimage.900.600.jpg" data-media="(min-width: 1024px)">
                      <img alt="Small lithium batteries" src="/content/dam/focal-point/cx/baggage/Small_lithium_batteries.renditionimage.900.600.jpg" role="presentation">
                    </span>
                    <noscript>
                      <img src="/content/dam/focal-point/cx/baggage/Small_lithium_batteries.renditionimage.900.600.jpg" alt="Small lithium batteries"/>
                    </noscript>
                  </span>
                </div>
                <div class="detail-column">
                  <div class="equal-height-watch content badge-inverted-white details" style="height: 822px;">
                    <h3 class="title">
                      
                      Any type of spare batteries (including lithium batteries, power banks, alkaline dry cells)
                    </h3>
                    <div class="description">
                      <p>Spare lithium batteries must under 100 Watt-hour (Wh) / 2g Lithium content (LC)</p>
<p>Examples:</p>
<ul>
<li>Cells for mobile phones</li>
<li>Cameras</li>
<li>Watches</li>
<li>Portable music players</li>
<li>Laptop computers.</li>
</ul>
<p><b>In cabin baggage</b></p>
<ul>
<li>20 spare pieces allocated per passenger</li>
<li>Must be presented correctly (either enclosed in original retail packaging, with the terminals taped over or each one placed in a separate plastic bag)</li>
</ul>
<p><b>In check in baggage</b></p>
<ul>
<li>Any type of spare batteries is strictly prohibited in checked baggage. This includes, but is not limited to, lithium, alkaline and dry cell batteries.</li>
</ul>
<p><b>Banned in baggage</b></p>
<ul>
<li>Non-rechargeable batteries with more than 2g of lithium (e.g. a ‘C’ size battery and above) are forbidden in any baggage and must be presented and carried as cargo following IATA Dangerous Goods regulations.</li>
</ul>

                    </div>
                  </div>
                </div>
              </div>
              
  

            </div>
          
            

            <div class="col-sm-12 col-md-4 col-lg-4">
              <div class="item">
                
                <div class="image-column">
                  <span data-picture="" data-role="presentation" data-alt="Medium lithium batteries">
                    <span data-src="/content/dam/focal-point/cx/baggage/Medium_lithium_batteries.renditionimage.900.600.jpg"></span>
                    
                    <span data-src="/content/dam/focal-point/cx/baggage/Medium_lithium_batteries.renditionimage.900.600.jpg" data-media="(min-width: 720px)" style="background-image: url('/content/dam/focal-point/cx/baggage/Medium_lithium_batteries.renditionimage.900.600.jpg');"></span>
                    <span data-src="/content/dam/focal-point/cx/baggage/Medium_lithium_batteries.renditionimage.900.600.jpg" data-media="(min-width: 1024px)">
                      <img alt="Medium lithium batteries" src="/content/dam/focal-point/cx/baggage/Medium_lithium_batteries.renditionimage.900.600.jpg" role="presentation">
                    </span>
                    <noscript>
                      <img src="/content/dam/focal-point/cx/baggage/Medium_lithium_batteries.renditionimage.900.600.jpg" alt="Medium lithium batteries"/>
                    </noscript>
                  </span>
                </div>
                <div class="detail-column">
                  <div class="equal-height-watch content badge-inverted-white details" style="height: 822px;">
                    <h3 class="title">
                      
                      Medium lithium batteries
                    </h3>
                    <div class="description">
                      <p>100 - 160 Watt-hour (Wh)</p>
<p>Examples:</p>
<ul>
<li>Extended life batteries for laptops</li>
<li>Batteries used by audio-visual professionals</li>
<li>portable medical devices such as Portable Oxygen Concentrators</li>
</ul>
<p><b>In cabin baggage</b></p>
<ul>
<li>2 spare pieces allocated per passenger&nbsp;</li>
<li>Must be presented correctly (either enclosed in original retail packaging, with the terminals taped over or each one placed in a separate plastic bag)</li>
</ul>
<p><b>In check in baggage</b></p>
<ul>
<li>Allowed inside equipment</li>
</ul>

                    </div>
                  </div>
                </div>
              </div>
              
  

            </div>
          
            

            <div class="col-sm-12 col-md-4 col-lg-4">
              <div class="item">
                
                <div class="image-column">
                  <span data-picture="" data-role="presentation" data-alt="Large lithium batteries">
                    <span data-src="/content/dam/focal-point/cx/baggage/Large_lithium_batteries_02.renditionimage.900.600.jpg"></span>
                    
                    <span data-src="/content/dam/focal-point/cx/baggage/Large_lithium_batteries_02.renditionimage.900.600.jpg" data-media="(min-width: 720px)" style="background-image: url('/content/dam/focal-point/cx/baggage/Large_lithium_batteries_02.renditionimage.900.600.jpg');"></span>
                    <span data-src="/content/dam/focal-point/cx/baggage/Large_lithium_batteries_02.renditionimage.900.600.jpg" data-media="(min-width: 1024px)">
                      <img alt="Large lithium batteries" src="/content/dam/focal-point/cx/baggage/Large_lithium_batteries_02.renditionimage.900.600.jpg" role="presentation">
                    </span>
                    <noscript>
                      <img src="/content/dam/focal-point/cx/baggage/Large_lithium_batteries_02.renditionimage.900.600.jpg" alt="Large lithium batteries"/>
                    </noscript>
                  </span>
                </div>
                <div class="detail-column">
                  <div class="equal-height-watch content badge-inverted-white details" style="height: 822px;">
                    <h3 class="title">
                      
                      Large lithium batteries
                    </h3>
                    <div class="description">
                      <p>160+ Watt-hour</p>
<p>Examples:</p>
<ul>
<li>Industry equipment, found in some electric and hybrid vehicles</li>
<li>Mobility devices and scooters</li>
</ul>
<p><b>Banned from baggage</b></p>
<ul>
<li>Must be presented and carried as cargo in accordance with <a href="http://www.iata.org/whatwedo/cargo/dgr/Pages/lithium-batteries.aspx">IATA Dangerous Goods Regulations</a></li>
</ul>
<p><b>Exceptions</b></p>
<ul>
<li>Lithium-ion battery powered wheelchairs or similar mobility aids used by passengers with restricted mobility due to health, age or temporary issues (for example, a broken leg).<br>
<br>
Please contact <a href="/content/cx/en_US/contact-us.html">Customer Care </a>for assistance.</li>
<br>
</ul>

                    </div>
                  </div>
                </div>
              </div>
              
  

            </div>
          
        
        
        
        
        
      </div>
    </div>
  </div>
</div>






    

</div>
<div class="text parbase section aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div class="cmp-text">
    <p>Please note that spare lithium batteries, also called “loose” batteries, are carried separately and used as backup to recharge lithium-ion batteries installed in mobile phones, laptop computers and other equipment. While spare lithium batteries, including portable battery chargers and power banks are permitted for use inside the cabin, it is strictly prohibited to recharge them using the in-seat power outlet or USB port at any time due to potential safety hazards.</p>
<p><br>
Please pack spare lithium batteries in your carry on luggage, following the guidelines above.&nbsp;</p>
<p><a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=jvxS3-0QzT4&amp;list=UU3ytY1MCWiwMiSyO414izow" target="_self">Watch this safety video from CASA</a>&nbsp;(Civil Aviation Safety Authority) to learn more about travelling with lithium batteries.<br>
</p>

</div>

    

</div>
<div class="accordion parbase aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">


		<div class="section-wrapper-bt accordion-standard connected ">
            <div class="container  ">
				<div class="panel-group" id="aid_10ffc80a-0789-48a3-a8e0-8ef3152935a5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_522308157" aria-multiselectable="false">
					 <div class="panel">
                     	<a class="panel-heading collapsed" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#aid_10ffc80a-0789-48a3-a8e0-8ef3152935a5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_522308157" href="#aid_10ffc80a-0789-48a3-a8e0-8ef3152935a5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_522308157-content" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="aid_10ffc80a-0789-48a3-a8e0-8ef3152935a5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_522308157-content" id="aid_10ffc80a-0789-48a3-a8e0-8ef3152935a5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_522308157-title">
                            <span class="label">Read our further guidelines for travel with lithium batteries</span>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-down"></i>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-up"></i>
						</a>
						<div id="aid_10ffc80a-0789-48a3-a8e0-8ef3152935a5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_522308157-content" class="panel-collapse collapse" aria-labelledby="aid_10ffc80a-0789-48a3-a8e0-8ef3152935a5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_522308157-title">
							<div class="responsivegrid">


<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
    
    <div class="text parbase section aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div class="cmp-text">
    <p>Please ensure that you have the information available for our staff when requested:<br>
<br>
1. The Watt-hour (Wh) or Lithium content (g) for all the installed and spare batteries that you are planning to bring either as carry-on or check-in baggage.</p>
<p>(You can work this out by using the following calculation:&nbsp;<br>
Amp-hours (Ah) to Watt-hours (Wh) Conversion: Multiply Ah by Voltage (V), (1Ah = 1,000 mAh), both of these data are displayed on the information plate of the battery.</p>
<p>Example: 2.38Ah x 14.4V = 34 Wh for a laptop computer lithium-ion battery)</p>
<p>Lithium batteries with no or unclear marking of Watt-hour (Wh) rating or Lithium Content (LC) will be refused carriage.</p>
<p>2. Must meet the United Nations (UN) test requirements specified in the&nbsp;<b>UN Manual of Tests and Criteria, Part III Section 38.3</b>.</p>
<p>3. Equipment and devices with built-in or plug-in lithium batteries – such as laptop computers, cameras, and mobile phones – must be completely switched off (not in sleep or hibernation mode), and with measures taken to ensure that they cannot be accidentally activated and are protected from damage when placed in check-in baggage.</p>
<p>4. The maximum number of equipment and electronic devices containing lithium batteries (each piece within 100Wh or 2g) for carriage in check-in baggage is&nbsp;<b>15 pieces</b>&nbsp;per passenger, and up to&nbsp;<b>15 pieces</b>&nbsp;in each bag. For example:</p>
<ul>
<li>15 pieces per passenger in total (e.g. one passenger checks in two bags)</li>
<li>15 pieces maximum in one bag (e.g. two passengers check in one bag only)</li>
</ul>
<p>5. For&nbsp;<b>US DOT regulations,</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;passengers travelling to and from the US with lithium batteries should visit&nbsp;<a href="http://phmsa.dot.gov/safetravel">www.phmsa.dot.gov/safetravel</a>&nbsp;for details.</p>
<p>6. Non-rechargeable batteries&nbsp;with more than 2 grams of lithium (like a ‘C’ size battery and above) are forbidden in any baggage and must be presented and carried as cargo in accordance with the<a href="http://www.iata.org/whatwedo/cargo/dgr/Pages/lithium-batteries.aspx">&nbsp;IATA dangerous goods</a>&nbsp;regulations.</p>
<p>7. Electronic cigarettes cannot be carried in checked baggage, and must not be used on board the aircraft.</p>

</div>

    

</div>

    
</div>
</div>

						</div>
					 </div>
				</div>
			</div>
		</div>
</div>
<div class="accordion parbase aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">


		<div class="section-wrapper-bt accordion-standard connected ">
            <div class="container  ">
				<div class="panel-group" id="aid_10ffc80a-0789-48a3-a8e0-8ef3152935a5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_310431067" aria-multiselectable="false">
					 <div class="panel">
                     	<a class="panel-heading collapsed" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#aid_10ffc80a-0789-48a3-a8e0-8ef3152935a5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_310431067" href="#aid_10ffc80a-0789-48a3-a8e0-8ef3152935a5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_310431067-content" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="aid_10ffc80a-0789-48a3-a8e0-8ef3152935a5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_310431067-content" id="aid_10ffc80a-0789-48a3-a8e0-8ef3152935a5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_310431067-title">
                            <span class="label">Ban on hoverboards and other self-balancing scooters</span>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-down"></i>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-up"></i>
						</a>
						<div id="aid_10ffc80a-0789-48a3-a8e0-8ef3152935a5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_310431067-content" class="panel-collapse collapse" aria-labelledby="aid_10ffc80a-0789-48a3-a8e0-8ef3152935a5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_310431067-title">
							<div class="responsivegrid">


<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
    
    <div class="text parbase section aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div class="cmp-text">
    <p><b>Please note: Small vehicles powered by lithium ion batteries are forbidden in passenger checked and cabin baggage.</b><br>
<br>
In view of the fire risk associated with small vehicles powered by lithium ion batteries – including the AirWheel, Solowheel, Hoverboards and mini Segways, and other self-balancing scooters – Cathay Pacific has announced a ban on the carriage of such vehicles and related accessories in both checked and cabin baggage on all Cathay Pacific flights with effect from 9 December 2015.<br>
<br>
Cathay Pacific passengers are not allowed to bring small vehicles running on lithium ion batteries onto the aircraft, per our guidelines. If these items are brought to the airport they will be refused at check-in, and it will be the passenger’s responsibility to arrange the disposal of such banned items prior to boarding. Cathay Pacific will not store these items due to the associated fire risk.</p>

</div>

    

</div>
<div class="image aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div data-cmp-is="image" data-cmp-lazythreshold="0" data-cmp-src="/content/cx/en_US/baggage/controlled-and-banned-items/lithium-batteries/_jcr_content/contentpar/contentblock/responsivegrid/accordion_310431067/accordion/image.coreimg{.width}.jpeg/1713321603545/ban-on-hoverboards-self-balancing-scooters.jpeg" data-asset="/content/dam/focal-point/cx/baggage/Ban-on-hoverboards-self-balancing-scooters.jpg" data-asset-id="dc1dea10-a6e3-4bca-8413-8c345a9dd386" id="image-e11513df09" class="cmp-image" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject">
    
        
            
            <img src="/content/cx/en_US/baggage/controlled-and-banned-items/lithium-batteries/_jcr_content/contentpar/contentblock/responsivegrid/accordion_310431067/accordion/image.coreimg.jpeg/1713321603545/ban-on-hoverboards-self-balancing-scooters.jpeg" class="cmp-image__image" itemprop="contentUrl" data-cmp-hook-image="image" alt="">
            
        
    
    
    
</div>

<div class="text parbase section aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div class="cmp-text">
    <p>Example:<br>
</p>
<ul>
<li>AirWheel</li>
<li>Solowheel</li>
<li>Hoverboards and mini Segways</li>
<li>Other self-balancing scooters</li>
</ul>

		</div>

<div class="accordion parbase aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">


		<div class="section-wrapper-bt accordion-standard ">
            <div class="container  ">
				<div class="panel-group" id="aid_10ffc80a-0789-48a3-a8e0-8ef3152935a5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1866720831" aria-multiselectable="false">
					 <div class="panel">
                     	<a class="panel-heading collapsed" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#aid_10ffc80a-0789-48a3-a8e0-8ef3152935a5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1866720831" href="#aid_10ffc80a-0789-48a3-a8e0-8ef3152935a5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1866720831-content" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="aid_10ffc80a-0789-48a3-a8e0-8ef3152935a5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1866720831-content" id="aid_10ffc80a-0789-48a3-a8e0-8ef3152935a5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1866720831-title">
                            <span class="label">Legal notice</span>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-down"></i>
							<i lang="en" aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon-arrow-up"></i>
						</a>
						<div id="aid_10ffc80a-0789-48a3-a8e0-8ef3152935a5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1866720831-content" class="panel-collapse collapse" aria-labelledby="aid_10ffc80a-0789-48a3-a8e0-8ef3152935a5_contentpar_contentblock_responsivegrid_accordion_1866720831-title">
							<div class="responsivegrid">


<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
    
    <div class="text parbase section aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div class="cmp-text">
    <p>We ask that all our passengers adhere to the above acceptance criteria when travelling with lithium batteries. And whilst we don't like to say no to our passengers, we will be forced to refuse carriage of any excessive and unacceptable batteries upon discovery.</p>
<p>On check in, our staff will ask you if you have read the lithium batteries regulations. It is a criminal offence to make a false statement in response to this question, punishable on conviction to a fine of HKD 10,000 and / or imprisonment for up to six months. We will also be forced to inform the police and airport security services. To avoid this, please take note of our guildlines.</p>
<p>Please note that your bags may be searched before and / or after check in, should this be necessary.</p>

</div>

|<div class="aem-container aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12"><div class="  aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12"><div class="c-grid container cmp-pageTitle container"><div class="row"><div class="col-4 col-m-8 col-l-9"><h1 class="heading cmp-pageTitle__title" data-heading="h1" style="box-sizing: border-box;">Change, cancel or refund your flight</h1></div></div></div><div></div></div><div class="  aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12"><div class="c-grid container cmp-columnControl"><div class="row"><div class="col-4 col-m-4 col-l-6"><div class=""><div class="aem-container aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12"><div class="  aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12"><div><div class="image container top-0"><div class="responsiveImage -withRatio" style="--imageWidth: 900; --imageHeight: 450; --imageWidthMD: 900; --imageHeightMD: 600; --imageWidthLG: 1700; --imageHeightLG: 1133;"><div><picture><source class="responsiveImage__img" media="(min-width: 905px)" srcset="https://www.cathaypacific.com/content/dam/focal-point/cx/membership/campaigns/campaign-sign-up-form/Manage%20booking.renditionimage.1700.1133.jpg"><source class="responsiveImage__img" media="(min-width: 600px) and (max-width: 904.98px)" srcset="https://www.cathaypacific.com/content/dam/focal-point/cx/membership/campaigns/campaign-sign-up-form/Manage%20booking.renditionimage.900.600.jpg"><img class="responsiveImage__img" src="https://www.cathaypacific.com/content/dam/focal-point/cx/membership/campaigns/campaign-sign-up-form/Manage booking.renditionimage.900.450.jpg" alt="Text"></picture></div></div></div></div><div></div></div></div><div></div></div></div><div class="col-4 col-m-4 col-l-6"><div class=""><div class="aem-container aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12"><div class="  aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12"><div class="c-grid container c-aem-text -default"><div class="row"><div class="col-4 col-m-8 col-l-9"><h2>Flexible ticket change options</h2>
<p>We understand travel plans can change. That’s why we want to provide you with as much flexibility and options to make changes to your ticket. Find out more about how to change, cancel or refund your booking.</p>
</div></div></div><div></div></div></div><div></div></div></div></div></div><div></div></div><div class="  aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12"><div class="cmp-pillarBlock -fullWidth" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><div class="cmp-pillarBlock__bgGradient" style="box-sizing: border-box; background-image: linear-gradient(rgb(241, 244, 241) 0%, white 100%);"></div><div class="c-grid container"><div class="row"><div class="col-4 col-m-8 col-l-12"><div style="box-sizing: border-box;"><div class="cmp-pillarBlock__item" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><div class="c-grid container cmp-pillarSectionHeading"><div class="row"><div class="col-4 col-m-8 col-l-9"><div class="cmp-pillarSectionHeading__superTitle" style="box-sizing: border-box;"></div><h2 class="heading cmp-pillarSectionHeading__title" data-heading="h2" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><div class="" style="box-sizing: border-box;"> </div></h2><div class="cmp-pillarSectionHeading__desc" style="box-sizing: border-box;"></div></div></div></div></div><div class="cmp-pillarBlock__item" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><div class=""><div class="aem-container aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12"><div class="  aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12"><div class="c-grid container c-aem-text -default"><div class="row"><div class="col-4 col-m-8 col-l-9"><h2><img src="/content/dam/focal-point/digital-library/svg-icons/icon3-0/default-dark-grey/travel/fligtchange.svg" alt="" width="40" style="vertical-align: middle;">&nbsp;&nbsp;Change a booking</h2>
</div></div></div><div></div></div><div class="  aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12"><div class="c-grid container c-aem-text -default"><div class="row"><div class="col-4 col-m-8 col-l-9"><h3>Eligibility</h3>
<p>For all tickets purchased through Cathay Pacific, date and flight changes can be made for an itinerary involving the same routes.*</p>
<p>For tickets purchased through a travel agent – please contact them directly to organise your change.</p>
<p><sub>* Rebooking may not be allowed or may incur additional fees. Subject to the fare rules of your ticket.</sub></p>
</div></div></div><div></div></div><div class="  aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12"><div class="c-grid container c-aem-text -default"><div class="row"><div class="col-4 col-m-8 col-l-9"><h3>How to change a booking</h3>
<p>If you booked through Cathay Pacific – on our website, mobile app or through Customer Care – the fastest way to make changes to your booking is to log into <a href="/content/cx/en_US/manage-booking/manage-booking.html">Manage Booking</a>. You can rebook your flights by clicking the “Change or cancel your flight” button.</p>
<p>Passengers under the same booking are required to change dates and/or flights together when changing flight bookings online.</p>
<p>If the itinerary involves connecting flights with other carriers, you’ll also be able to make changes to your booking.</p>
<p>If you booked a redemption ticket, you can change your travel date for a fee of USD50 or <img src="/content/dam/focal-point/digital-library/svg-icons/dark-grey/asiamiles-currency.svg" alt="Asia Miles" style="max-width: 10px;">7,500 through <a href="/content/cx/en_US/manage-booking/manage-booking.html">Manage Booking</a> prior to your original departure and ticket expiry date. A booking and ticketing service fee will also apply if changed through other channels.*</p>
<p>If you booked through a travel agent, you can make changes to your booking for a fee of USD60/HKD470 by contacting Customer Care.</p>
<p><sub>* Changes are subject to award seat availability.</sub></p>
</div></div></div><div></div></div><div class="  aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12"><div class="c-grid container c-aem-text -default"><div class="row"><div class="col-4 col-m-8 col-l-9"><h3>Will I be charged a rebooking fee?</h3>
<p>A rebooking fee may apply depending on <a href="/content/cx/en_US/flights/fare-classes.html">the fare type</a> you have purchased.</p>
<p>You may also be required to pay the fare difference* due to changes in fare conditions including:</p>
<ul>
<li>Duration of stay</li>
<li>Availability of the fare class in your original booking</li>
<li>Seasonality and peak travel period surcharges on the rebooked dates</li>
</ul>
<p><sub>* Passengers will not be entitled to fare refunds in case of a fare reduction except in certain markets<br>
</sub></p>
</div></div></div><div></div></div><div class="  aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12"><div class="c-grid container cmp-link margin-bottom-40 margin-top-0"><div class="row"><div class="col-4 col-m-8 col-l-12 -buttonPositionLeft"><a class="c-link -button" data-variant="secondary-button" target="_self" href="https://www.cathaypacific.com/cx/en_US/manage-booking/manage-booking.html">Login to change your booking</a></div></div></div><div></div></div></div><div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div></div></div><div class="  aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12"><div class="cmp-pillarBlock -fullWidth" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><div class="cmp-pillarBlock__bgGradient" style="box-sizing: border-box; background-image: linear-gradient(rgb(241, 244, 241) 0%, white 100%);"></div><div class="c-grid container"><div class="row"><div class="col-4 col-m-8 col-l-12"><div style="box-sizing: border-box;"><div class="cmp-pillarBlock__item" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><div class="c-grid container cmp-pillarSectionHeading"><div class="row"><div class="col-4 col-m-8 col-l-9"><div class="cmp-pillarSectionHeading__superTitle" style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(0, 93, 99);"></div><h2 class="heading cmp-pillarSectionHeading__title" data-heading="h2" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><div class="" style="box-sizing: border-box;">  </div></h2><div class="cmp-pillarSectionHeading__desc" style="box-sizing: border-box;"></div></div></div></div></div><div class="cmp-pillarBlock__item" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><div class=""><div class="aem-container aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12"><div class="  aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12"><div class="c-grid container c-aem-text -default"><div class="row"><div class="col-4 col-m-8 col-l-9 margin-bottom-0"><h2><img src="/content/dam/focal-point/digital-library/svg-icons/icon3-0/default-dark-grey/lifestyle/moneydollar.svg" alt="" width="40" style="vertical-align: middle;">&nbsp;&nbsp;Cancellations and refunds</h2>
</div></div></div><div></div></div><div class="  aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12"><div class="c-grid container c-aem-text -default"><div class="row"><div class="col-4 col-m-8 col-l-9"><h3>How can I cancel or refund my ticket?</h3>
<p>If you booked through Cathay Pacific – on our website, mobile app or through Customer Care – the fastest way to cancel or organise a refund is to log into <a href="/content/cx/en_US/manage-booking/manage-booking.html">Manage Booking</a>. You can rebook your flights by clicking the “Change or cancel your flight” button.</p>
<p>If you purchased your ticket through a travel agent – please contact them directly to organise your cancellation. We are unable to process refunds for these bookings.</p>
<p>Partially used tickets that qualify for a refund will be credited back to the original payment credit card or bank account charged. *</p>
<p>If you booked a redemption ticket, you may cancel a completely unused ticket for a fee of USD120 or <img src="/content/dam/focal-point/digital-library/svg-icons/dark-grey/asiamiles-currency.svg" alt="Asia Miles" style="max-width: 10px;">17,000 by log into <a href="/content/cx/en_US/manage-booking/manage-booking.html">Manage Booking</a> prior to your ticket expiry date. The Asia Miles balance used to claim the award will then be credited to your account. Airport taxes and fuel surcharges will be refunded to the original payment credit card.</p>
<p><sub>* Subject to fare rules.</sub></p>
</div></div></div><div></div></div><div class="  aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12"><div class="c-grid container c-aem-text -default"><div class="row"><div class="col-4 col-m-8 col-l-9"><h3>Do I need to pay a cancellation fee?</h3>
<p>If you’d like to cancel your flight, a cancellation fee may apply depending on the fare type you have purchased.</p>
<p>For partially used tickets, you may be refunded the sectors that have not been flown after the cancellation fee and applicable tax/surcharges are deducted.<br>
</p>
</div></div></div><div></div></div><div class="  aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12"><div class="c-grid container c-aem-text -default"><div class="row"><div class="col-4 col-m-8 col-l-9"><h3>Refund processing time</h3>
<p>It normally takes up to 7 calendar days for us to process your refund request.</p>
<p>However, if your booking includes interline flights or more information is needed to process your refund (i.e. credit card used for the purchase has expired and your bank account details are needed instead), the processing time will take longer.</p>
<p>Please note that the time required for the actual refund to reach your account will depend on individual banks and payment service providers.</p>
</div></div></div><div></div></div><div class="  aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12"><div class="c-grid container c-aem-text -default"><div class="row"><div class="col-4 col-m-8 col-l-9 margin-bottom-0"><h3>24-hour free cancellation</h3>
<p>Cathay members who purchased their ticket directly through Cathay Pacific – on our website or mobile app – can cancel their ticket free of charge* within 24 hours through <a href="/content/cx/en_US/manage-booking/manage-booking.html">Manage Booking</a>. Visit <a href="/content/cx/en_US/membership/24-hour-free-cancellation.html">24-hour free cancellation</a> to learn more.</p>
</div></div></div><div></div></div><div class="  aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12"><div class="c-grid container cmp-link margin-bottom-40 margin-top-0"><div class="row"><div class="col-4 col-m-8 col-l-12 -buttonPositionLeft"><a class="c-link -button" data-variant="secondary-button" target="_self" href="https://www.cathaypacific.com/cx/en_US/manage-booking/manage-booking.html">Login to cancel and refund your booking</a></div></div></div><div></div></div></div><div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div></div></div><div class="  aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12"><div class="cmp-pillarBlock -fullWidth" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><div class="cmp-pillarBlock__bgGradient" style="box-sizing: border-box; background-image: linear-gradient(rgb(241, 244, 241) 0%, white 100%);"></div><div class="c-grid container"><div class="row"><div class="col-4 col-m-8 col-l-12"><div style="box-sizing: border-box;"><div class="cmp-pillarBlock__item" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><div class="c-grid container cmp-pillarSectionHeading"><div class="row"><div class="col-4 col-m-8 col-l-9"><div class="cmp-pillarSectionHeading__superTitle" style="box-sizing: border-box;"></div><h2 class="heading cmp-pillarSectionHeading__title" data-heading="h2" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><div class="" style="box-sizing: border-box;">  </div></h2><div class="cmp-pillarSectionHeading__desc" style="box-sizing: border-box;"></div></div></div></div></div><div class="cmp-pillarBlock__item" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><div class=""><div class="aem-container aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12"><div class="  aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12"><div class="c-grid container c-aem-text -default"><div class="row"><div class="col-4 col-m-8 col-l-9 margin-bottom-0"><h2><img src="/content/dam/focal-point/digital-library/svg-icons/icon3-0/default-dark-grey/travel/selfservice.svg" alt="" width="40" style="vertical-align: middle;">&nbsp; Refund status</h2>
</div></div></div><div></div></div><div class="  aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12"><div class="c-grid container c-aem-text -default"><div class="row"><div class="col-4 col-m-8 col-l-9"><h3>How can I check my refund status?</h3>
<p>If you purchased your ticket directly through Cathay Pacific and have submitted your refund requests through Manage Booking, the online refund form or Customer Care, you can log into <a href="/content/cx/en_US/manage-booking/manage-booking.html">Manage Booking</a> to check your refund status for the past 90 days.</p>

    <div class="page-title parbase section">
<div class="container   ">
        
        
            
                
                
	
    
        <div class="section-wrapper-bt green-title-grey-description">
            <div class="container   ">
                <div class="abstract">
                    <div class="wrapper">
                        
                            
                            
                                <div class="breadcrumbs">
                                    <div><a></a></div>
                                </div>
                            
                        
                        
                        <div class="wrapper">
                            <h1 class="title">Flight delay and cancellation</h1>
                            
                                <div class="description">
                                    
                                        We understand how stressful a flight delay or cancellation can be and we at Cathay Pacific will always do our best to minimise the impact to your journey. On this page, you can learn how to receive updates and information about your travel arrangements when your flight is delayed or cancelled.
                                    
                                    
                                </div>
                            
                            
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
    

            
            
        
    
</div>

</div>

    
  

    
    
  
    
    
    <div class="holder-fluid section">
    <div class="content-block section parbase   ">
    	
    	<div>


<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
    
    <div class="contentlist parbase holder-fluid aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">









  




<div class="content-list">
  <div class="section-wrapper-bt section parbase  content-list-index-icon ">
    <div class="container   ">
      <h2 class="caption">What to do if your flight is disrupted</h2>
      

      <div class="row equal-height">
        
        
          
            <div class="col-sm-12 col-md-12 col-lg-12 icon-list">
              <img class="icon" src="/content/dam/focal-point/digital-library/svg-icons/jade/information.svg" alt="Get the latest information">
              <div class="equal-height-watch content badge-inverted-grey details" style="">
                <h3 class="title">Get the latest information</h3>
                <div class="description">
                  <p></p><p>In the case of flight disruptions, we will provide regular updates to our customers. Please check the <b>Travel alerts</b> posted on the homepage for the latest updates. You can also check <a href="/content/cx/en_US/prepare-trip/flight-status.html">Flight status</a> on our website.</p>
<p>If you are already at the airport, you can check the latest updates via the <b>screens</b> or <b>public announcements</b>. Cathay Pacific airport agents are always there for assistance.</p>
<p></p>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
          
            <div class="col-sm-12 col-md-12 col-lg-12 icon-list">
              <img class="icon" src="/content/dam/focal-point/digital-library/svg-icons/jade/cellular_data.svg" alt="Provide contact information">
              <div class="equal-height-watch content badge-inverted-grey details" style="">
                <h3 class="title">Provide contact information</h3>
                <div class="description">
                  <p></p><p>Please ensure that your contact information is accurate within <a href="/content/cx/en_US/manage-booking.html">Manage booking</a>, to receive the latest updates. Customers can sign up for <i><b>notiFLY</b></i> mobile text messages (SMS), to be alerted of changes to flight status. This is especially helpful when internet access is not available. Note that, if you change your mobile phone SIM card while travelling, notiFLY text messages will not be delivered.</p>
<p></p>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
          
            <div class="col-sm-12 col-md-12 col-lg-12 icon-list">
              <img class="icon" src="/content/dam/focal-point/digital-library/svg-icons/jade/check_in.svg" alt="Manage your booking">
              <div class="equal-height-watch content badge-inverted-grey details" style="">
                <h3 class="title">Manage your booking</h3>
                <div class="description">
                  <p></p><p>Subject to the nature of the flight cancellation, we will issue special ticketing guidelines ahead of a flight disruption allowing for passengers to make changes to their booking free of charge.</p>
<p>Customers who booked via cathaypacific.com or Cathay Pacific mobile app, who wish to change their travel arrangements, may do so via <a href="/content/cx/en_US/manage-booking.html">Manage booking</a>, subject to the special ticketing guidelines issued for your flight rebooking – the guidelines will be linked to from the Travel alert when available.</p>
<p>Customers who booked through a travel agent should contact their booking agent for assistance first.</p>
<p>If your flight is cancelled, or missed due to disruption delay, <b>we’ll do our best to automatically rebook you onto the next available flight,</b> within the same cabin originally purchased. Your new flight details will be reflected within <a href="/content/cx/en_US/manage-booking.html">Manage booking</a>. Note that, if the number of affected customers is particularly high, we may take time to process your new travel arrangements.</p>
<p></p>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
          
            <div class="col-sm-12 col-md-12 col-lg-12 icon-list">
              <img class="icon" src="/content/dam/focal-point/digital-library/svg-icons/jade/airport.svg" alt="Before you go to the airport">
              <div class="equal-height-watch content badge-inverted-grey details" style="">
                <h3 class="title">Before you go to the airport</h3>
                <div class="description">
                  <p></p><p>If you receive information that your flight has been delayed or cancelled, please&nbsp;<b>do not proceed to the airport</b>&nbsp;for the originally scheduled flight.</p><p>If your flight has been delayed, and there is a new estimated time of departure, the check-in and boarding times will reflect the new departure time.</p><p>If your flight has been cancelled and you have a new flight arrangement, please note the new check-in and boarding times.</p><p>In circumstances where flight disruptions are due to local weather, we suggest checking with your local transportation options on any delays or cancellations that may affect your journey to the airport.</p><p></p>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
          
        
        

        
        
        

        
        
        
        
        
        
      </div>
    </div>
  </div>
</div>






    

</div>
<div class="text parbase section aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div class="cmp-text">
    <p><b>Note: To understand your passenger rights in the event of a flight delay or cancellation, please refer to the</b> <a href="/content/cx/en_US/prepare-trip/passenger-rights-and-regulations.html">Passenger Rights and Regulations</a> <b>page.</b></p>

</div>

    

</div>
